#-Empire War Events
namespace = empire_wars
# original event chain written by knuckey and blackninja
# adapted to Warhammer: Gehemnisnacht by Komioski
#-Main events
#-----------
#[empire_wars.1 - .3] - King is at war with an Elector Count/Independant realm, calls Elector Counts Levies
#[empire_wars.4] - Vassal  king/Elector Count has empire title flag set immediately
#[empire_wars.5] - Rebel leader assigned flags and call levies if possible
#[empire_wars.6] - Grand Theoginist seeks refuge in your capital
#[empire_wars.7] - Elector Count responds
#[empire_wars.8] - Civil war ending event (King, triggered from on_action and MTTH)
#[empire_wars.901 & 9] - Inform king/Elector Count of war end- re-vassalised if applicable, or post civil wars flag set
#[empire_wars.900] - Inform lord of war end- re-vassalised if applicable, or post civil wars flag set
#[empire_wars.10 - .11] - Sort out Grand Theoginist refuge
#[empire_wars.12] - Lord is re-vassalised after their post civil war wars are done
#[empire_wars.13] - Lord supporting king rejoins King's war if at peace
#[empire_wars.14 - .18] - Lord is defending against external realm post civil war- King decides to help or not
#[empire_wars.19] - Crown Loyalist joins King
#[empire_wars.20] - Liege Loyalist follows Liege

#Vassal control events
#-----------------------
#[empire_wars.21-22] - AI Mid War Control
#[empire_wars.23] - On death vassal inherit control
#[empire_wars.24] - King/Elector Count tier inherit/yearly decision
#[empire_wars.25] - Vassal of King/Elector Count initial response
#[empire_wars.26] - Vassal of King/Elector Count  inherit/yearly decision

#Inform character events
#----------------------
#[empire_wars.30 - .40 ]

#Flag maintenance
#----------------------
#[empire_wars.41] - Diplomatic call to arms set flags
#[empire_wars.42] - Maintain defacto opinion link with split vassal
#[empire_wars.4299] - Vassal of split vassal rebels, add defacto liege link to Emperor
#[empire_wars.43] - Flag maintenance
#[empire_wars.44] - on_create_title , reset defacto Empire variables

#Independence Events
#----------------------
#[empire_wars.50] - Elector Count/King wins indep war
#[empire_wars.51] - A Lord that wins independance from Elector Count/King during civil chooses whether to swear fealty to Emperor (triggered from indep CB in cb_types)
#[empire_wars.52] - Character loses dejure kingdom war against King, assign flag to revassalise (from cb_types)
#[empire_wars.53] - Indep War Victory Ally Maintenance
#[empire_wars.54] - Small AI lords in successful independence faction attach to larger ally

#empire_wars War Drama
#-----------------------
#[empire_wars.60 - .73] - My close relative is opposing my host
#[empire_wars.74 - 85] - Emperor deals with defeated rebels/traitors
#[empire_wars.86-  95] - Rebel Leader resolution, deals with defeated Emperor
#[empire_wars.96-  100] - Vassal is harbouring exiled pretender

#Maintaining the council
#-----------------------
#[empire_wars.101 - 103] - Reappoint the old council members

 #Game start maintenance events
 character_event = { #set title variables
	 id = mega_wars.999

	 is_triggered_only = yes
	 hide_window = yes
	 #only_rulers = yes

	 trigger = {
		 has_landed_title = e_rebels
		 NOT = { has_global_flag = scenario_initialised }
	 }

	 immediate = {
		 set_global_flag = scenario_initialised
		 #Set mega war title law flags
		 e_rebels = { set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 2 } } #e_rebels counts how many empires have been flagged
		 e_the_empire = { set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } }

		 e_rebels = { set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 15 } } #e_rebels counts how many kingdoms have been flagged
		 k_cult_of_sigmar = { set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 1 } }
		 k_reikland = { set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 2 } }
		 k_averland = { set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 3 } }
		 k_hochland = { set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 4 } }
		 k_middenland = { set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 5 } }
		 k_mootland = { set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 6 } }
		 k_nordland = { set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 7 } }
		 k_ostermark = { set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 8 } }
		 k_ostland = { set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 9 } }
		 k_stirland = { set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 10 } }
		 k_sylvania = { set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 11 } }
		 k_talabecland = {set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 12 } }
		 k_westerland = { set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 13 } }
		 k_wissenland = { set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 14 } }

		 character_event = { id = mega_wars.998 days = 1 }
	 }

	 option = {
		 name = OK
	 }
 }
 character_event = { #give flags to ruler designer characters
	 id = mega_wars.998

	 is_triggered_only = yes
	 hide_window = yes

	 trigger = { has_landed_title = e_rebels }

	 immediate = {
		 any_playable_ruler = {
			 limit = {
				 ai = no
			 }
			 if = {
				 limit = {
					 NOT = { trait = civil_war }
					 NOT = { trait = rebel_leader }
					 NOT = { has_character_flag = supporting_king }
					 NOT = { has_character_flag = neutral }
					 NOT = { has_character_flag = against_king }
					 OR = {
						 AND = {
							 independent = yes
							 primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } }
						 }
						 liege = {
							 OR = {
								 trait = civil_war
								 trait = rebel_leader
								 has_character_flag = supporting_king
								 has_character_flag = neutral
								 has_character_flag = against_king
							 }
						 }
					 }
				 }
				 set_character_flag = neutral
			 }
		 }
	 }

	 option = {
		 name = OK
	 }
 }

###Main Event Series###
#King is at war with an Elector Count, calls Elector Count levies
character_event = { #If triggered from on_actions, makes sure King is FROMFROM scope
	id = empire_wars.1

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_game_rule = {
				name = empire_wars
				value = off
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = { #Check defender
			limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
			character_event = { id = empire_wars.3 }
		}
		FROM = { #Check attacker
			if = {
				limit = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
				}
				character_event = { id = empire_wars.2 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.2

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		tier = EMPEROR
	}

	immediate = {
		character_event = { id = empire_wars.3 }
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.3
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.3"
	picture = GFX_evt_empirewar

	hide_from = yes
	only_independent = yes
	war = yes

	trigger = {
		tier = EMPEROR
		OR = { #Only trigger for nomads if they have non-nomad vassals, vassal nomad clans will not be split
			is_nomadic = no
			any_vassal = { tier = KING is_nomadic = no }
		}
		NOT = {
			has_game_rule = {
				name = empire_wars
				value = off
			}
		}
		NOT = { crownlaw_title = { has_law = centralization_4 } } #Disabled on max authority
		NOT = { rebel_leader = { has_character_modifier = new_rebel_leader is_alive = yes war_with = ROOT } } #Only one new rebel leader can be considered at a time
		NOT = { has_character_flag = considering_surrender } #Do not trigger if still considering surrender to a dragon conquest
		NOT = { government = alliance_government } #Does not apply to alliance governments
		any_vassal = { higher_tier_than = BARON } #actually has vassals
		OR = { #Does not apply to Elector kingdoms in an independence war
			primary_title = { NOT = { has_title_flag = indep_war } }
			NOT = {
				any_war = {
					attacker = { character = ROOT }
					OR = {
						using_cb = bid_for_independence
						using_cb = cb_faction_independence
					}
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			any_demesne_title = { #One of the empire tier titles is being contested
				tier = EMPEROR
				any_war = {
					attacker = {
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
						NOT = { trait = rebel_leader }
						NOT = { has_character_flag = considering_surrender }
					}
				}
			}
			any_war = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						defender = { character = ROOT }
						attacker = {
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
							NOT = { has_character_flag = considering_surrender }
							OR = {
								AND = { #Vassal attacker only trigger empire war if either...
									OR = {
										tier = KING #King tier
										has_character_flag = indep_war #declaring independence
										PREV = { using_cb = overthrow_ruler } #Is in war of tyranny
									}
									liege_before_war = { character = ROOT }
									NOT = { trait = rebel_leader }
									war_with = ROOT
									#liege = { character = ROOT }
								}
								AND = { #External Attackers
									NOT = { trait = rebel_leader }
									war_with = ROOT
									liege_before_war = { character = PREV }
									OR = { #Musn't be landless (with some exceptions)
										demesne_size = 1
										has_character_flag = claimant_adventurer
										has_character_flag = duchy_adventurer
										has_character_flag = religious_revolter
									}
									NOT = { liege = { character = ROOT }	}
									ROOT = { is_primary_war_defender = yes }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						attacker = { character = ROOT }
						defender = {
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
							NOT = { has_character_flag = considering_surrender }
							OR = {
								AND = { #King tier vassals always trigger empire war
									NOT = { trait = rebel_leader }
									war_with = ROOT
									OR = {
										tier = KING
										has_character_flag = indep_war
									}
									independent = no
									#liege = { character = ROOT }
								}
								AND = { #External Defenders
									OR = {
										NOT = { trait = rebel_leader }
										AND = { #Enemy emperors may already have the rebel_leader trait
											tier = EMPEROR
											NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_emperor_rebel_leader } }
										}
									}
									war_with = ROOT
									liege_before_war = { character = PREV }
									demesne_size = 1
									NOT = { liege = { character = ROOT }	}
									ROOT = { is_primary_war_attacker = yes }
									NOT = { has_character_flag = crownlander_resists }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			any_playable_ruler = { #Enemies who have the support of a king tier vassal trigger an empire war
				NOT = { trait = rebel_leader }
				tier = KING
				NOT = { liege_before_war = { character = PREV } }
				OR = {
					liege_before_war = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { liege = { tier = EMPEROR } }
				}
				war_with = ROOT
				any_war = {
					OR = {
						attacker = { character = ROOT }
						defender = { character = ROOT }
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_character_flag = against_king }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = inherit_war }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = considering_surrender }
				NOT = {
					any_war = {
						OR = {
							attacker = { trait = rebel_leader }
							defender = { trait = rebel_leader }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		##Make sure empire title has a unique variable set
		e_rebels = {
			ROOT = {
				primary_title = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } } }
						set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }
						e_rebels = { change_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } }
					}
				}
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						NOT = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } }
					}
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }
					e_rebels = { change_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { trait = civil_war } }
				# Flag councillors
				any_opinion_modifier_target = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_castellan }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_chancellor }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_marshal }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_treasurer }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_spymaster }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_learned }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_priest }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_ships }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_admiral }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_commander }
						}
					}
					reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_castellan }
					reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_chancellor }
					reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_marshal }
					reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_treasurer }
					reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_spymaster }
					reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_learned }
					reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_priest }
					reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_ships }
					reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor }
					reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_admiral }
					reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_commander }
				}
				job_castellan = {
					if = {
						limit = { is_ruler = yes }
						reverse_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_castellan
							months = 240
						}
						add_character_modifier = { name = not_fired_from_council duration = 10 hidden = yes }
					}
				}
				job_chancellor = {
					if = {
						limit = { is_ruler = yes }
						reverse_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_chancellor
							months = 240
						}
						add_character_modifier = { name = not_fired_from_council duration = 10 hidden = yes }
					}
				}
				job_marshal = {
					if = {
						limit = { is_ruler = yes }
						reverse_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_marshal
							months = 240
						}
						add_character_modifier = { name = not_fired_from_council duration = 10 hidden = yes }
					}
				}
				job_treasurer = {
					if = {
						limit = { is_ruler = yes }
						reverse_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_treasurer
							months = 240
						}
						add_character_modifier = { name = not_fired_from_council duration = 10 hidden = yes }
					}
				}
				job_spymaster = {
					if = {
						limit = { is_ruler = yes }
						reverse_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_spymaster
							months = 240
						}
						add_character_modifier = { name = not_fired_from_council duration = 10 hidden = yes }
					}
				}
				job_physician = {
					if = {
						limit = { is_ruler = yes }
						reverse_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_learned
							months = 240
						}
						add_character_modifier = { name = not_fired_from_council duration = 10 hidden = yes }
					}
				}
				job_spiritual = {
					if = {
						limit = { is_ruler = yes }
						reverse_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_priest
							months = 240
						}
						add_character_modifier = { name = not_fired_from_council duration = 10 hidden = yes }
					}
				}
				random_courtier_or_vassal = {
					limit = {
						is_ruler = yes
						has_minor_title = title_high_admiral
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_admiral
						months = 240
					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = not_fired_from_council duration = 10 hidden = yes }
				}
				random_courtier_or_vassal = {
					limit = {
						is_ruler = yes
						has_minor_title = title_high_admiral_B
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_admiral
						months = 240
					}
				}
				any_courtier_or_vassal = {
					limit = {
						is_ruler = yes
						has_minor_title = title_small_council_advisor
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor
						months = 240
					}
				}
				random_courtier_or_vassal = {
					limit = {
						is_ruler = yes
						has_minor_title = title_councilmember_king
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor
						months = 240
					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = not_fired_from_council duration = 10 hidden = yes }
				}
				random_courtier_or_vassal = {
					limit = {
						is_ruler = yes
						has_minor_title = title_councilmember_emperor
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor
						months = 240
					}
					add_character_modifier = { name = not_fired_from_council duration = 10 hidden = yes }
				}
				any_courtier_or_vassal = {
					limit = {
						is_ruler = yes
						has_minor_title = title_commander
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_commander
						months = 240
					}
				}
			}
		}
		##Flags
		add_trait = civil_war
		clr_global_flag = war_cooldown_period
		clr_character_flag = supporting_king
		clr_character_flag = neutral
		clr_character_flag = against_king
		clr_character_flag = rebel_leader
		clr_character_flag = post_civil_war_wars
		clr_character_flag = independant
		clr_character_flag = join_independance_asked
		hidden_tooltip = {
			#Flag Crown Loyalists
			random_vassal = {
				limit = { leads_faction = faction_crown_loyalist }
				set_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_crown_loyalist
					set_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist
				}
			}
			any_vassal = {
				limit = { tier = KING }
				random_vassal = {
					limit = { leads_faction = faction_crown_loyalist }
					set_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist
					any_faction_backer = {
						faction = faction_crown_loyalist
						set_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist
					}
				}
			}
		}
		character_event = { id = maintenance.51 } #crown law maintenance

		##Find rebel leader and flag them
		hidden_tooltip = {
			clear_event_target = new_rebel_leader
			random_current_enemy = { #for war leaders claiming the empire
				limit = {
					NOT = { trait = rebel_leader }
					NOT = { has_character_flag = considering_surrender }
					ROOT = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = EMPEROR
							any_war = {
								attacker = {
									character = PREVPREVPREVPREV
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = { set_character_flag = rebel_leader_found }
				save_event_target_as = new_rebel_leader
				character_event = { id = empire_wars.5 } #set rebel leader flags
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = rebel_leader_found } }
				random_playable_ruler = { #for war leaders that aren't king tier but allied with a King tier
					limit = {
						liege = {
							tier = KING
							NOT = { liege_before_war = { character = PREV } }
							war_with = ROOT
							#NOT = { liege = { war_with = ROOT } }
							any_war = {
								OR = {
									attacker = { character = ROOT }
									defender = { character = ROOT }
								}
								NOT = {
									OR = {
										attacker = { tier = KING }
										defender = { tier = KING }
									}
								}
								NOT = {
									OR = {
										attacker = { trait = rebel_leader }
										defender = { trait = rebel_leader }
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					liege = {
						any_war = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									attacker = { character = ROOT }
									defender = { character = ROOT }
								}
								NOT = {
									OR = {
										attacker = { tier = KING }
										defender = { tier = KING }
									}
								}
								NOT = {
									OR = {
										attacker = { trait = rebel_leader }
										defender = { trait = rebel_leader }
									}
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = { attacker = { character = ROOT } }
								defender = {
									save_event_target_as = new_rebel_leader
									ROOT = { set_character_flag = rebel_leader_found }
									character_event = { id = empire_wars.5 } #set rebel leader flags
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = { defender = { character = ROOT } }
								attacker = {
									save_event_target_as = new_rebel_leader
									ROOT = { set_character_flag = rebel_leader_found }
									character_event = { id = empire_wars.5 } #set rebel leader flags
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = rebel_leader_found } }
				any_war = { #for LP tier
					limit = {
						OR = {
							attacker = { character = ROOT }
							defender = { character = ROOT }
						}
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								attacker = { trait = rebel_leader NOT = { character = ROOT } }
								defender = {
									trait = rebel_leader
									OR = { #Enemy emperors may already have the rebel_leader trait
										NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
										has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_emperor_rebel_leader }
									}
									NOT = { character = ROOT }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							attacker = {
								war_with = ROOT
								NOT = { trait = rebel_leader }
								OR = {
									AND = { #Vassal attacker only trigger empire war if either...
										OR = {
											tier = KING #King tier
											has_character_flag = indep_war #declaring independence
											PREV = { using_cb = overthrow_ruler } #Is in war of tyranny
										}
										liege_before_war = { character = ROOT }
										#liege = { character = ROOT }
									}
									AND = {
										liege_before_war = { character = PREV }
										OR = {
											demesne_size = 1
											has_character_flag = claimant_adventurer
											has_character_flag = duchy_adventurer
											has_character_flag = religious_revolter
										}
										NOT = { liege = { character = ROOT }	}
									}
								}
								is_primary_war_attacker = yes
							}
						}
						attacker = {
							save_event_target_as = new_rebel_leader
							ROOT = { set_character_flag = rebel_leader_found }
							character_event = { id = empire_wars.5 } #set rebel leader flags
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							defender = {
								war_with = ROOT
								OR = {
									NOT = { trait = rebel_leader }
									AND = { #Enemy emperors may already have the rebel_leader trait
										tier = EMPEROR
										NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_emperor_rebel_leader } }
									}
								}
								OR = {
									AND = {
										tier = KING
										liege_before_war = { character = ROOT }
										#liege = { character = ROOT }
									}
									AND = {
										liege_before_war = { character = PREV }
										demesne_size = 1
										NOT = { liege = { character = ROOT }	}
										NOT = { has_character_flag = crownlander_resists }
									}
								}
								is_primary_war_defender = yes
							}
						}
						defender = {
							save_event_target_as = new_rebel_leader
							ROOT = { set_character_flag = rebel_leader_found }
							character_event = { id = empire_wars.5 } #set rebel leader flags
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = rebel_leader_found } }
				any_independent_ruler = { #External Attackers
					limit = {
						war_with = ROOT
						is_primary_war_attacker = yes
						OR = {
							demesne_size = 1
							has_character_flag = claimant_adventurer
							has_character_flag = duchy_adventurer
							has_character_flag = religious_revolter
						}
						NOT = { liege_before_war = { character = ROOT }	}
						ROOT = { is_primary_war_defender = yes }
						NOT = { trait = rebel_leader }
					}
					save_event_target_as = new_rebel_leader
					ROOT = { set_character_flag = rebel_leader_found }
					character_event = { id = empire_wars.5 } #set rebel leader flags
				}
			}
			#If no rebel leader found try FROM and FROMFROM scopes as last resort
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = rebel_leader_found } }
				FROM = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							war_with = ROOT
							OR = {
								NOT = { trait = rebel_leader }
								AND = { #Enemy emperors may already have the rebel_leader trait
									tier = EMPEROR
									NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_emperor_rebel_leader } }
								}
							}
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
						}
						ROOT = { set_character_flag = rebel_leader_found }
						save_event_target_as = new_rebel_leader
						character_event = { id = empire_wars.5 } #set rebel leader flags
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = rebel_leader_found } }
				FROMFROM = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							war_with = ROOT
							OR = {
								NOT = { trait = rebel_leader }
								AND = { #Enemy emperors may already have the rebel_leader trait
									tier = EMPEROR
									NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_emperor_rebel_leader } }
								}
							}
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
						}
						ROOT = { set_character_flag = rebel_leader_found }
						save_event_target_as = new_rebel_leader
						character_event = { id = empire_wars.5 } #set rebel leader flags
					}
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = rebel_leader_found
		}

		##Call the Elector Count/King tier's levies
		#Immediately break king tier vassals so their levies cannot be used
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				tier = KING
				is_nomadic = no
				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				war = no
				NOT = {
					liege = {
						tier = EMPEROR
					}
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_landed_title = k_cult_of_sigmar }
					ROOT = {
						crownlaw_title = {
							OR = {
								has_law = investiture_law_2
								has_law = investiture_law_3
							}
						}
					}
				}
				has_character_flag = neutral
				NOT = { has_character_flag = issue_punishments }
				primary_title = {
					ROOT = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = EMPEROR
							is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }
							check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist } }
				letter_event = { id = empire_wars.7 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPempire_wars.7 }
			}
			if = { #Crown Loyalists
				limit = { has_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist }
				character_event = { id = empire_wars.19 days = 1 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPempire_wars.7 }
			}
		}
		any_vassal = {
			limit = {
				tier = KING
				war = no
				OR = {
					is_patrician = no #dont break republic
					is_merchant_republic = yes
				}
				is_nomadic = no
				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = issue_punishments }
				NOT = { #not split when outside force is claiming title
					any_realm_title = {
						any_war = {
							attacker = {
								NOT = { is_liege_or_above = ROOT }
							}
						}
						#holder_scope = { war = yes }
					}
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_landed_title = k_cult_of_sigmar }
					ROOT = {
						crownlaw_title = {
							OR = {
								has_law = investiture_law_2
								has_law = investiture_law_3
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = empire_wars.4 } } #set empire title flag

			opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege years = 25 }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist } }
				set_character_flag = empire_war_remove_leader
				letter_event = { id = empire_wars.7 days = 1 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPempire_wars.7 }
			}
			if = { #Crown Loyalists
				limit = { has_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist }
				set_character_flag = empire_war_remove_leader
				character_event = { id = empire_wars.19 days = 1 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPempire_wars.7 }
			}
		}

		character_event = { id = empire_wars.60 days = 30 } #find held courtiers related to enemies/rebels

		#Lower tier vassal banners called (counts/dukes)
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tier = KING }
					NOT = { tier = BARON }
					NOT = { war_with = root }
					war = no
					NOT = { #not split when outside force is claiming title
						any_realm_title = {
							any_war = {
								attacker = {
									NOT = { is_liege_or_above = ROOT }
								}
							}
							#holder_scope = { war = yes }
						}
					}
					primary_title = {
						mercenary = no
						holy_order = no
					}
				}
				#opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_deciding_king days = 10 }
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist } }
					letter_event = { id = empire_wars.25 days = 2 }
				}
				if = { #Crown Loyalists
					limit = { has_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist }
					character_event = { id = empire_wars.19 days = 2 }
				}
			}
			remove_character_modifier = empire_war_no_levies
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.3"
		tooltip = {
			any_independent_ruler = { #Call the Elector Counts Levies
				limit = {
					tier = KING
					NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					war = no
					has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
				}
				custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPempire_wars.7 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTempire_warsTOOLTIP"
		trigger = { ai = no }
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPempire_warsTOOLTIP }
	}
}
#Vassal  king/Elector Count has empire title flag set immediately
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.4

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = independant
		FROM = { set_empire_war_empire_variable_ROOT_effect = yes }
		any_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tier = COUNT
					tier = DUKE
				}
			}
			set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
#Rebel leader assigned flags and call levies if possible
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.5

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = independant

		#Make sure kingdom title has a unique variable set
		if = {
			limit = { tier = KING }
			e_rebels = {
				ROOT = {
					primary_title = {
						if = {
							limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 1 } } }
							set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" which = PREVPREV }
							e_rebels = { change_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 1 } }
						}
					}
					any_demesne_title = {
						limit = {
							tier = KING
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 1 } }
						}
						set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" which = PREVPREV }
						e_rebels = { change_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 1 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		#Make sure empire title has a unique variable set
		if = {
			limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
			e_rebels = {
				ROOT = {
					primary_title = {
						if = {
							limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } } }
							set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }
							e_rebels = { change_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } }
						}
					}
					any_demesne_title = {
						limit = {
							tier = EMPEROR
							NOT = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } }
						}
						set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }
						e_rebels = { change_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}

		if = { #If emperor who already has the rebel_leader trait add an extra flag to show empire wars has triggered
			limit = {
				trait = rebel_leader
				tier = EMPEROR
				NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_emperor_rebel_leader } }
			}
			opinion = {
				who = FROM
				modifier = opinion_emperor_rebel_leader
				years = 25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					AND = {
						liege = { character = ROOT }
						NOT = {
							liege_before_war = {
								character = FROM
								NOT = { character = ROOT }
							}
						}
						primary_title = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } } }	#no defacto empire
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					primary_title = { has_title_flag = indep_war }
				}
				OR = { #Does not apply to kingdoms in an independence war
					NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
					primary_title = { NOT = { has_title_flag = indep_war } }
					NOT = {
						any_war = {
							attacker = { character = ROOT }
							OR = {
								using_cb = bid_for_independence
								using_cb = cb_faction_independence
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = independant
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_character_flag = independant }
				NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
				NOT = { liege_before_war = { NOT = { character = FROM } } }
				OR = {
					primary_title = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } } } #independent
					NOT = { #Make sure rebel isnt actually part of another empire
						any_independent_ruler = {
							tier = EMPEROR
							NOT = { character = FROM }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
							any_demesne_title = {
								tier = EMPEROR
								check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
								ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_defacto_liege = THIS
			FROM = { set_empire_war_empire_variable_ROOT_effect = yes }
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tier = COUNT
						tier = DUKE
					}
				}
				set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0 }
			}
		}
		clr_character_flag = neutral
		clr_character_flag = supporting_king
		clr_character_flag = against_king
		set_character_flag = rebel_leader
		add_trait = rebel_leader
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = "new_rebel_leader"
			duration = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_character_flag = independant }
				tier = KING
			}
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					NOT = { tier = BARON }
					war = no
					NOT = { #not split when outside force is claiming title
						any_realm_title = {
							any_war = {
								attacker = {
									NOT = { is_liege_or_above = FROM }
									NOT = { is_liege_or_above = ROOT }
								}
							}
							#holder_scope = { war = yes }
						}
					}
					primary_title = {
						mercenary = no
						holy_order = no
					}
				}
				set_character_flag = event_triggered_from_rebel_leader
				#opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_deciding_king days = 10 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist }
						NOT = { in_faction = faction_liege_loyalist }
					}
					letter_event = { id = empire_wars.25 days=1 }
				}
				if = { #Crown Loyalists
					limit = { has_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist }
					character_event = { id = empire_wars.19 days=1 }
				}
				if = { #Liege Loyalists
					limit = { in_faction = faction_liege_loyalist }
					character_event = { id = empire_wars.20 days=1 }
				}
			}
		}

		#If Grand Theoginist is rebel leader maybe seek refuge in another rebel's capital
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_landed_title = k_cult_of_sigmar
				is_theocracy = yes
				NOT = { num_of_count_titles = 1 }
				capital_scope = { owner = { character = FROM } }
			}
			random_playable_ruler = { #Find King tier first
				limit = {
					liege = {
						war_with = FROM
						NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
						religion = sigmarite
						tier = KING ###
						OR = {
							liege_before_war = { character = FROM }
							AND = {
								war_with = FROM
								has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
							}
						}
						any_vassal = {
							tier = BARON
							religion = sigmarite
							is_theocracy = yes
						}
					}
				}
				liege = {
					character_event = { id = empire_wars.6 }
					ROOT = { set_character_flag = refuge_found }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = refuge_found } }
				random_playable_ruler = {
					limit = {
						liege = {
							war_with = FROM
							NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
							religion = sigmarite
							OR = {
								liege_before_war = { character = FROM }
								AND = {
									war_with = FROM
									has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
								}
							}
							any_vassal = {
								tier = BARON
								religion = sigmarite
								is_theocracy = yes
							}
						}
					}
					liege = { character_event = { id = empire_wars.6 } }
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = refuge_found
		}

		character_event = { id = empire_wars.60 days = 30 } #find held courtiers related to enemies/rebels
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
#Inform Grand Theoginist seeks refuge in your capital
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.6
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.6"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.6"
		random_vassal = {
			limit = {
				tier = BARON
				religion = sigmarite
				is_theocracy = yes
			}
			random_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					tier = BARON
					holding_type = temple
				}
				gain_title = FROM
				set_title_flag = grand_theoginist_refuge
				FROM = { capital = PREV }
			}
		}
		FROM = { opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_gave_refuge months = 120 } }
		piety = 200
		FROM = {
			hidden_tooltip = {
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = { location = { owner = { character = FROMFROM } } }
					set_title_flag = grand_theoginist_capital
					gain_title = FROMFROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
#Elector Count responds
letter_event = {
	id = empire_wars.7
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.7"

	is_triggered_only = yes
	war = no

	trigger = {
		tier = KING
		is_nomadic = no
		NOT = { war_with = FROM }
		FROM = { war = yes }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = being_issued_punishment }
		NOT = { #not split when outside force is claiming title
			any_realm_title = {
				any_war = {
					attacker = {
						NOT = { is_liege_or_above = FROM }
					}
				}
				#holder_scope = { war = yes }
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_landed_title = k_cult_of_sigmar }
			FROM = {
				crownlaw_title = {
					OR = {
						has_law = investiture_law_2
						has_law = investiture_law_3
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		###Set Empire Title Law 'Flag'###

		#Make sure kingdom title has a unique variable set
		e_rebels = {
			ROOT = {
				primary_title = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 1 } } }
						set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" which = PREVPREV }
						e_rebels = { change_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 1 } }
					}
				}
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						tier = KING
						NOT = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 1 } }
					}
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" which = PREVPREV }
					e_rebels = { change_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}

		clr_character_flag = independant
		set_character_flag = empire_war_remove_leader
		clr_character_flag = must_decide
		clr_character_flag = joined_independance_war
		set_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
		if = { #If granted kingdom reset empire war flags
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_granted_kingdom
					}
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			clr_character_flag = neutral
		}
		if = { #Check Elector Count Status
			limit = { FROM = { FROM = { has_landed_title = e_the_empire } }	}
			if = { #Elector Count
				limit = {
					has_landed_title = k_reikland
					event_target:new_rebel_leader = {

				}

		clr_character_flag = against_king
		clr_character_flag = inherit_war
		clr_character_flag = empire_war_remove_leader
		hidden_tooltip = { set_defacto_liege = THIS }
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = elector_called_to_arms	}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = TOOLTIPELECTOREMPIREWARWARNING
				hidden_tooltip = {
					any_playable_ruler = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_liege_or_above = ROOT
								is_liege_or_above = FROM
								primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } } #The Empire
							}
						}
						opinion = { modifier = opinion_bad_elector who = ROOT years = 10 }
					}
				}
			}
			prestige = -400
			FROM = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_elector_no_defend
					who = ROOT
					years = 10
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = elector_called_to_arms
		}
		FROM = {
			reverse_war = {
				target = ROOT
				casus_belli = bid_for_independence
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { letter_event = { id = empire_wars.35 days=1 } }
		}
		event_target:new_rebel_leader = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_allied_with = ROOT
						has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = broke_alliance
					who = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_allied_with = ROOT
						has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = broke_alliance
					who = ROOT
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_dynasty_loyalist }
				}
				ROOT = {
					change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = maintenance.3 } }#dishonour trait
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { war_with = root }
					war = no
					primary_title = {
						mercenary = no
						holy_order = no
					}
					NOT = { tier = BARON }
				}
				clr_character_flag = supporting_king
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				clr_character_flag = against_king
				# clr_character_flag = rebel_leader
				# clr_character_flag = post_civil_war_wars
				# clr_character_flag = independant
				# clr_character_flag = join_independance_asked
				# clr_character_flag = inherit_war
				#opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_deciding_king days = 10 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist }
						NOT = { in_faction = faction_liege_loyalist }
					}
					letter_event = { id = empire_wars.25 days=3 }
				}
				if = { #Crown Loyalists
					limit = { has_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist }
					character_event = { id = empire_wars.19 days=3 }
				}
				if = { #Liege Loyalists
					limit = { in_faction = faction_liege_loyalist }
					character_event = { id = empire_wars.20 days=3 }
				}
			}
			FROM = { #opinion malus with all opponents
				any_war = {
					limit = {
						defender = { character = ROOT_FROM }
					}
					any_defender = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy } }
							NOT = { character = ROOT_FROM }
						}
						opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
					}
				}
				any_war = {
					limit = {
						attacker = { character = ROOT_FROM }
					}
					any_attacker = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy } }
							NOT = { character = ROOT_FROM }
						}
						opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTempire_warsTOOLTIP"
		trigger = { ai = no }
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPempire_warsTOOLTIP }
		hidden_tooltip = { repeat_event = { id = empire_wars.7 } }
	}
}
#War ends (The Empire)
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.8
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.8"
	picture = GFX_evt_battle

	only_independent = yes

	trigger = {
		tier = EMPEROR
		trait = civil_war
		OR = {
			war = no
			# FROM = {
				# has_character_flag = rebel_leader
			# }
			NOR = {
				any_demesne_title = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					any_war = {
						attacker = {
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							#trait = rebel_leader
							#NOT = { has_character_flag = considering_surrender }
						}
					}
				}
				any_war = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							defender = { character = ROOT }
							attacker = {
								NOT = { character = ROOT }
								NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
								#NOT = { has_character_flag = considering_surrender }
								OR = {
									AND = { #Vassal attacker only trigger empire war if either...
										OR = {
											tier = KING #King tier
											has_character_flag = indep_war #declaring independence
											PREV = { using_cb = overthrow_ruler } #Is in war of tyranny
										}
										liege_before_war = { character = ROOT }
										war_with = ROOT
										#liege = { character = ROOT }
									}
									AND = { #External Attackers
										war_with = ROOT
										liege_before_war = { character = PREV }
										OR = { #Musn't be landless (with some exceptions)
											demesne_size = 1
											has_character_flag = claimant_adventurer
											has_character_flag = duchy_adventurer
											has_character_flag = religious_revolter
										}
										NOT = { liege = { character = ROOT }	}
										ROOT = { is_primary_war_defender = yes }
									}
									trait = rebel_leader
								}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							attacker = { character = ROOT }
							defender = {
								NOT = { character = ROOT }
								NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
								#NOT = { has_character_flag = considering_surrender }
								OR = {
									AND = { #King tier vassals always trigger empire war
										war_with = ROOT
										OR = {
											tier = KING
											has_character_flag = indep_war
										}
										independent = no
										#liege = { character = ROOT }
									}
									AND = { #External Defenders
										war_with = ROOT
										liege_before_war = { character = PREV }
										demesne_size = 1
										NOT = { liege = { character = ROOT }	}
										ROOT = { is_primary_war_attacker = yes }
									}
									trait = rebel_leader
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				any_playable_ruler = { #Enemies who have the support of a king tier vassal trigger an empire war
					tier = KING
					NOT = { liege_before_war = { character = PREV } }
					OR = {
						liege_before_war = { character = ROOT }
						NOT = { liege = { tier = EMPEROR } }
					}
					war_with = ROOT
					any_war = {
						OR = {
							attacker = { character = ROOT }
							defender = { character = ROOT }
						}
					}
					NOT = { has_character_flag = against_king }
					NOT = { has_character_flag = inherit_war }
					#NOT = { has_character_flag = considering_surrender }
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = issue_punishments }
			had_character_flag = { flag = issue_punishments days = 7 }
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			remove_trait = civil_war
			clr_character_flag = harsh_justice
			clr_character_flag = issue_punishments
			clr_character_flag = supporting_king
			clr_character_flag = neutral
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			clr_character_flag = rebel_leader
			clr_character_flag = independant
			clr_character_flag = join_independance_asked
			clr_character_flag = no_kingship
			remove_trait = rebel_leader
			clr_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
			any_opinion_modifier_target = {
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader }
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_with_king }
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_emperor_rebel_leader }
			}
			any_opinion_modifier_target = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						independent = no
						war = no
					}
				}
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
			}
			#Sort out Grand Theoginist refuge
			k_cult_of_sigmar = {
				holder_scope = {
					character_event = { id = empire_wars.10 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_landed_title = e_the_empire
					ai = yes
					NOT = { has_global_flag = altdorf_not_capital }
					capital_scope = { NOT = { province_id = 299 } }
					has_landed_title = b_kaiserliche_palast
				}
				b_kaiserliche_palast = {
					ROOT = { capital = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.8"
		hidden_tooltip = {
			#Re-absorb king tier vassals
			any_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					tier = KING
					is_nomadic = no
					NOT = { has_character_flag = independant }
					NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					primary_title = {
						ROOT = {
							any_demesne_title = {
								tier = EMPEROR
								is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }
							}
						}
						check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_character_flag = independant }
						NOT = { has_character_flag = joined_independance_war }
					}
					character_event = { id = empire_wars.9 days = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = joined_independance_war
					}
					set_character_flag = post_civil_war_wars
				}
			}
			#Clear flags from lower vassals
			any_realm_lord = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tier = COUNT
						tier = DUKE
					}
				}
				clr_character_flag = empire_war_remove_leader
				clr_character_flag = issue_punishments
				clr_character_flag = inherit_war
				clr_character_flag = supporting_king
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				clr_character_flag = against_king
				clr_character_flag = against_liege
				clr_character_flag = rebel_leader
				clr_character_flag = independant
				clr_character_flag = join_independance_asked
				clr_character_flag = no_kingship
				clr_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
				remove_trait = rebel_leader
				any_opinion_modifier_target = {
					reverse_remove_opinion = { who = PREV modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader }
					reverse_remove_opinion = { who = PREV modifier = opinion_with_king }
					reverse_remove_opinion = { who = PREV modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege	}
				}
				character_event = { id = empire_wars.900 days = 2 }
			}
			#Reabsorb split vassals
			any_independent_ruler = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tier = COUNT
						tier = DUKE
					}
					primary_title = {
						ROOT = {
							any_demesne_title = {
								tier = EMPEROR
								is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }
							}
						}
						check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = empire_wars.900 days = 2 }
			}
			#Clear flags
			any_independent_ruler = {
				limit = {
					trait = rebel_leader
					war = no
				}
				remove_trait = rebel_leader
				clr_character_flag = rebel_leader
			}
			remove_trait = rebel_leader

			###Post empire war events
			character_event = { id = maintenance.51 days = 3 } #crown law maintenance
			character_event = { id = maintenance.52 days = 3 } # Empire AI vassal limit management
			set_character_flag = empire_war_reappointing_council
			character_event = { id = empire_wars.101 days = 3 } # Reappoint council
			character_event = { id = faction_event_new.90 } #recalculate fear modifier
			character_event = { id = interregnum.1 days = 7 } #check for interregnum
			any_vassal = { #check for new merchant republics
				limit = {
					is_republic = yes
					higher_tier_than = BARON
					is_merchant_republic = no
					is_government_potential = merchant_republic_government
				}
				set_government_type = merchant_republic_government
				if = {
					limit = { is_patrician = no }
					create_family_palace = yes
				}
			}
			any_vassal = {
				limit = { is_merchant_republic = yes }
				character_event = { id = REP.908 }
			}
			##

		}
	}
}
#Inform king/Elector Count of war end
character_event = { #continuously check all king tier character
	id = empire_wars.901

	only_independent = yes
	hide_window = yes

	trigger = {
		tier = KING
		is_nomadic = no
		NOT = { has_character_flag = independant }
		primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } }
		any_independent_ruler = {
			tier = EMPEROR
			war = no
			NOT = { trait = civil_war }
			any_demesne_title = {
				tier = EMPEROR
				ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
				check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = joined_independance_war }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = post_civil_war_wars }
	}

	immediate = {
		character_event = { id = empire_wars.9 }
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
character_event = { #triggered from both MTTH event above and emperor's war ending event
	id = empire_wars.9
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.9"
	picture = GFX_evt_battle

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tier = KING
		is_nomadic = no
	}

	immediate = {
		any_war = { #External wars of conquest against high rank titles are invalidated
			limit = {
				attacker = { character = ROOT }
				defender = {
					NOR = {
						same_realm = ROOT
						any_demesne_title = {
							ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
							check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
						}
					}
				}
				thirdparty_title_scope = { NOT = { lower_tier_than = ROOT } }
				OR = {
					using_cb = claim
					using_cb = invasion
					using_cb = tribal_invasion
					using_cb = invasion_ambition
					using_cb = unjust_conquest
				}
			}
			end_war = invalid
		}
		set_character_flag = no_kingship
		clr_character_flag = will_be_reabsorbed
		clr_character_flag = empire_war_remove_leader
		clr_character_flag = end_indep_wars
		clr_character_flag = issue_punishments
		any_realm_lord = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tier = COUNT
					tier = DUKE
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = empire_war_remove_leader
			clr_character_flag = issue_punishments
			clr_character_flag = inherit_war
			clr_character_flag = supporting_king
			clr_character_flag = neutral
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			clr_character_flag = against_liege
			clr_character_flag = rebel_leader
			clr_character_flag = independant
			clr_character_flag = join_independance_asked
			clr_character_flag = no_kingship
			clr_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
			remove_trait = rebel_leader
			any_opinion_modifier_target = {
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = PREV modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader }
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = PREV modifier = opinion_with_king }
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = PREV modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege	}
			}
			character_event = { id = empire_wars.900 days = 5 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_landed_title = k_cult_of_sigmar }
			character_event = { id = empire_wars.10 }
		}
		any_vassal = { #mark vassals, to get around bug where vassals are removed temporarily
			set_character_flag = vassal_of_@ROOT
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.8" #Yes
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_character_flag = empire_wars_disabled #game rule
				war = no
			}
			NOT = { any_opinion_modifier_target = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_granted_independence } } }
			NOT = {
				liege = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					NOT = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = EMPEROR
							ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
							check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		random_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				tier = EMPEROR
				NOT = { trait = civil_war }
				OR = {
					war = no
					character = FROM #this means it was triggered by the emperor
					ROOT = { has_character_flag = empire_wars_disabled }
				}
				any_demesne_title = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
					check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
				}
			}
			if = { #Check for granting of independence
				limit = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_granted_independence } }
				hidden_tooltip = {
					ROOT = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							limit = { NOT = { tier = BARON } NOT = { tier = EMPEROR } }
							set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
						}
						any_realm_lord = {
							any_demesne_title = {
								limit = { NOT = { tier = BARON } NOT = { tier = EMPEROR } }
								set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
							}
						}
						clr_character_flag = supporting_king
						clr_character_flag = neutral
						clr_character_flag = against_king
						clr_character_flag = rebel_leader
						clr_character_flag = independant
						clr_character_flag = join_independance_asked
						clr_character_flag = no_kingship
						remove_trait = rebel_leader
						clr_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
						any_opinion_modifier_target = {
							remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader }
							remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_with_king }
							remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege	}
						}
						recalc_succession = yes
					}
				}
				break = yes
			}
			empire_war_merchant_republic_check_effect = yes
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { liege = { character = PREVPREV } } }
					set_defacto_liege = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = empire_war_regent }
			clr_character_flag = empire_war_regent
			if = {
				limit = {
					liege = {
						has_regent = yes
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
				}
				gain_regency_effect = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			liege = {
				#Make sure any vassals wrongly gained by liege are taken back
				any_vassal = {
					limit = {
						lower_tier_than = ROOT
						NOT = { tier = BARON }
						primary_title = {
							ROOT = {
								any_demesne_title = {
									tier = KING
									check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0.9 }
									is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" which = PREVPREV }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				}
				any_vassal = {
					limit = { has_character_flag = vassal_of_@ROOT }
					set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				}
			}

			clr_character_flag = supporting_king
			clr_character_flag = neutral
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			clr_character_flag = rebel_leader
			clr_character_flag = independant
			clr_character_flag = join_independance_asked
			clr_character_flag = no_kingship
			remove_trait = rebel_leader
			clr_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
			clr_character_flag = empire_wars_disabled
			any_opinion_modifier_target = {
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader }
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_with_king }
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege	}
			}
			recalc_succession = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBempire_wars.8" #Our war continues
		trigger = {
			war = yes
			NOT = { has_character_flag = empire_wars_disabled } #game rule
			NOT = { any_opinion_modifier_target = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_granted_independence } } }
			NOT = {
				liege = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					NOT = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = EMPEROR
							ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
							check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		#hidden_tooltip = {
			set_character_flag = post_civil_war_wars
			any_war = {
				limit = {
					using_cb = bid_for_independence
					defender = { character = ROOT }
				}
				attacker = { set_character_flag = post_civil_war_indep_war }
			}
		#}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege years = 25 }
			clr_character_flag = supporting_king
			clr_character_flag = neutral
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			clr_character_flag = rebel_leader
			clr_character_flag = independant
			clr_character_flag = join_independance_asked
			clr_character_flag = no_kingship
			remove_trait = rebel_leader
			clr_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
			any_opinion_modifier_target = {
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader }
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_with_king }
			}
			character_event = { id = interaction.899 days = 3 } #ask liege for help?
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTDempire_wars.8" #I was granted independence
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				liege = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					NOT = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = EMPEROR
							ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
							check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
						}
					}
				}
				any_opinion_modifier_target = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_granted_independence } }
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = { NOT = { tier = BARON } NOT = { tier = EMPEROR } }
				set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
			}
			any_realm_lord = {
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = { NOT = { tier = BARON } NOT = { tier = EMPEROR } }
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = supporting_king
			clr_character_flag = neutral
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			clr_character_flag = rebel_leader
			clr_character_flag = independant
			clr_character_flag = join_independance_asked
			clr_character_flag = no_kingship
			remove_trait = rebel_leader
			clr_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
			any_opinion_modifier_target = {
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader }
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_with_king }
				remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege	}
			}
			recalc_succession = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_tooltip = { any_vassal = { clr_character_flag = vassal_of_@ROOT } }
	}
}
#Inform neutral Elector Count vassal of war end
character_event = { #check lower tier characters at peace every year
	id = empire_wars.903

	is_triggered_only = yes
	only_independent = yes
	hide_window = yes
	war = no

	trigger = {
		lower_tier_than = KING
		NOT = { has_character_flag = independant }
		NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
		primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } }
		any_independent_ruler = {
			tier = EMPEROR
			war = no
			NOT = { trait = civil_war }
			any_demesne_title = {
				tier = EMPEROR
				ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
				check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = joined_independance_war }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = post_civil_war_wars }
	}

	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = empire_wars_disabled
		character_event = { id = empire_wars.900 }
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.900
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.9"
	picture = GFX_evt_battle

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } }
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				any_demesne_title = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					ROOT = {
						primary_title = {
							lower_tier_than = EMPEROR
							is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }
						}
					}
					check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
				}
			}
			has_character_flag = empire_wars_disabled
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = empire_war_remove_leader
		clr_character_flag = issue_punishments
		any_war = { #End all slave raids on this lord
			limit = {
				using_cb = slave_raid
				defender = { character = ROOT }
			}
			end_war = invalid
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.8" #Yes
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				war = no
				NOT = { independent = yes }
				has_character_flag = empire_wars_disabled
			}
			NOT = { any_opinion_modifier_target = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_granted_independence } } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { independent = yes }
			if = {
				limit = {
					primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 1 } }
					lower_tier_than = KING
					NOT = { liege = { character = FROM } }
				}
				random_playable_ruler = {
					limit = {
						higher_tier_than = DUKE
						any_demesne_title = {
							higher_tier_than = DUKE
							ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" which = PREVPREV } } }
							check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0.9 }
						}
					}
					empire_war_merchant_republic_check_effect = yes
					ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV }
					recalc_succession = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					independent = yes
				}
				random_independent_ruler = {
					limit = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = EMPEROR
							ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
							check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
						}
					}
					empire_war_merchant_republic_check_effect = yes
					ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV }
					recalc_succession = yes
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			clr_character_flag = inherit_war
			clr_character_flag = supporting_king
			clr_character_flag = neutral
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			clr_character_flag = against_liege
			clr_character_flag = rebel_leader
			clr_character_flag = independant
			clr_character_flag = join_independance_asked
			clr_character_flag = no_kingship
			clr_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
			remove_trait = rebel_leader
			clr_character_flag = empire_wars_disabled
			any_opinion_modifier_target = {
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader }
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_with_king }
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege	}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBempire_wars.8" #Our war continues
		trigger = {
			war = yes
			independent = yes
			NOT = { has_character_flag = empire_wars_disabled }
			NOT = { any_opinion_modifier_target = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_granted_independence } } }
		}
		#hidden_tooltip = {
			set_character_flag = post_civil_war_wars
			any_war = {
				limit = { 	using_cb = bid_for_independence
							defender = { character = ROOT }
				}
				attacker = { set_character_flag = 	post_civil_war_indep_war }
			}
		#}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege	years = 25 }
			clr_character_flag = supporting_king
			clr_character_flag = neutral
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			clr_character_flag = against_liege
			clr_character_flag = rebel_leader
			clr_character_flag = independant
			clr_character_flag = join_independance_asked
			clr_character_flag = no_kingship
			remove_trait = rebel_leader

			character_event = { id = interaction.899 days = 3 } #ask liege for help?
		}
	}

	option = {

#Sort out Grand Theoginist refuge
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.10

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	war = no

	trigger = {
		has_landed_title = k_cult_of_sigmar
	}

	immediate = {
		#Take back original temples
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				liege = {
					any_realm_title = {
						tier = BARON
						holding_type = temple
						has_title_flag = grand_theoginist_capital
					}
				}
			}
			liege = {
				random_realm_title = {
					limit = {
						tier = BARON
						holding_type = temple
						has_title_flag = grand_theoginist_capital
					}
					gain_title = ROOT
					clr_title_flag = grand_theoginist_capital
				}
			}
		}
		#Give refuge back to province owner
		random_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				tier = BARON
				holding_type = temple
				has_title_flag = grand_theoginist_refuge
			}
			location = {
				owner = {
					character_event = { id = empire_wars.11 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { name = OK }
}

#post civil war wars Elector Counts vassalage
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.12
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.12"
	picture = GFX_evt_powerful_ruler

	only_independent = yes
	war = no

	trigger = {
		has_character_flag = post_civil_war_wars
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			has_character_flag = joined_independance_war
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_landed_title = k_cult_of_sigmar }
			character_event = { id = empire_wars.10 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tier = KING }
			any_vassal = { #mark vassals, to get around bug where vassals are removed temporarily
				set_character_flag = vassal_of_@ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.12" #Yes
		clr_character_flag = post_civil_war_wars
		clr_character_flag = joined_independance_war
		clr_character_flag = will_be_reabsorbed
		clr_character_flag = empire_war_remove_leader
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = joined_vassal_tyranny_rebellion }
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					liege = {
						higher_tier_than = ROOT
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
					}
				}
				liege = {
					ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV }
				}
				recalc_succession = yes
			}
			clr_character_flag = joined_vassal_tyranny_rebellion
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				independent = yes
				lower_tier_than = KING
				primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 1 } }
			}
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					liege = {
						higher_tier_than = DUKE
						any_demesne_title = {
							higher_tier_than = DUKE
							ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" which = PREVPREV } } }
							check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0.9 }
						}
					}
				}
				liege = {
					empire_war_merchant_republic_check_effect = yes
					ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV }
				}
				recalc_succession = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				independent = yes
			}
			random_independent_ruler = {
				limit = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					any_demesne_title = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
						check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NAND = {
							trait = civil_war
							war = yes
						}
					}
					empire_war_merchant_republic_check_effect = yes
					ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						trait = civil_war
						war = yes
					}
					custom_tooltip = {
						text = TOOLTIPempire_wars.12A
					}
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = empire_wars.13 } } #check if they should rejoin king
					if = {
						limit = { ai = yes }
						character_event = { id = empire_wars.21 days = 1 } #ai choose sides
					}
				}
				recalc_succession = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { independent = yes } }
				liege = {
					reverse_remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
					any_vassal = { #Make sure any vassals wrongly gained by liege are taken back
						limit = {
							lower_tier_than = ROOT
							NOT = { tier = BARON }
							primary_title = {
								ROOT = {
									any_demesne_title = {
										tier = KING
										check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0.9 }
										is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" which = PREVPREV }
									}
								}
							}
						}
						set_defacto_liege = ROOT
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { tier = KING }
					liege = {
						any_vassal = {
							limit = { has_character_flag = vassal_of_@ROOT }
							set_defacto_liege = ROOT
						}
					}
					any_vassal = { clr_character_flag = vassal_of_@ROOT }
				}
				clr_character_flag = supporting_king
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				clr_character_flag = against_king
				clr_character_flag = against_liege
				clr_character_flag = rebel_leader
				clr_character_flag = independant
				clr_character_flag = join_independance_asked
				clr_character_flag = no_kingship
				any_opinion_modifier_target = {
					remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader }
					remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_with_king }
					remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
				}
			}
			remove_trait = rebel_leader
			clr_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
			clr_character_flag = inherit_war
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.13
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.13"
	picture = GFX_evt_empirewar

	only_independent = yes

	trigger = {
		#has_global_flag = empire_civil_war
		#tier = KING
		#independent = yes
		is_nomadic = no
		civil_war = {
			tier = EMPEROR
			is_alive = yes
			war = yes
			reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_with_king
			}
			NOT = {
				any_war = {
					OR = {
						attacker = {
							#trait = rebel_leader
							war_with = ROOT
						}
						defender = {
							#trait = rebel_leader
							war_with = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			any_war = {
				OR = {
					attacker = {
						trait = rebel_leader
						NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					}
					defender = {
						trait = rebel_leader
						NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_primary_war_attacker = yes
				is_primary_war_defender = yes
			}
		}
		OR = {
			has_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist
			has_character_flag = supporting_king
		}
		# NOT = {
			# any_war = {
				# OR = {
					# attacker = {
						# has_landed_title = e_the_empire
					# }
					# defender = {
						# has_landed_title = e_the_empire
					# }
				# }
			# }
		# }
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.13" #Yes
		clr_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist
		civil_war = {
			limit = {
				tier = EMPEROR
				is_alive = yes
				war = yes
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_with_king
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_primary_war_defender = yes
					any_war = {
						attacker = { trait = rebel_leader }
						defender = { character = PREVPREV }
					}
				}
				ROOT = { join_defender_wars = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_primary_war_attacker = yes
					any_war = {
						defender = { trait = rebel_leader }
						attacker = { character = PREVPREV }
					}
				}
				ROOT = { join_attacker_wars = PREV }
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { #failsafe
				ROOT = {
					join_defender_wars = PREV
					join_attacker_wars = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
#Lord is defending against external realm post civil war- King decides to help or not , triggered by decision
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.14

	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = { #If granted independence diplomatically cancel this
			limit = { any_opinion_modifier_target = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_granted_independence } } }
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tier = BARON }
					NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
				}
				set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
			}
			break = yes
		}
		if = { #First try and find king tier liege
			limit = {
				lower_tier_than = KING
				NOT = { has_character_flag = against_loyal_liege }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = against_rebel_liege }
				primary_title = {
					check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
					check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0.9 }
				}
			}
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					liege = {
						higher_tier_than = DUKE
						any_demesne_title = {
							higher_tier_than = DUKE
							ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" which = PREVPREV } } }
							check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0.9 }
						}
						NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					}
				}
				liege = { character_event = { id = empire_wars.15 days = 1 } }
				break = yes
			}
		}
		random_independent_ruler = { #Then try emperor tier liege
			limit = {
				tier = EMPEROR
				any_demesne_title = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
					check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
				}
				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
			}
			character_event = { id = empire_wars.15 days = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.15"
	picture = GFX_evt_empirewar

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.15" #Yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 97
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { is_primary_war_defender = yes }
			}
			FROM = {
				ROOT = {
					join_defender_wars = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = { letter_event = { id = empire_wars.16 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBempire_wars.15" #No
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				opinion = { who = FROM value = 0 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -50 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -75 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = arbitrary
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = deceitful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = slothful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = just
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = honorable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = honest
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = diligent
			}
		}
		prestige = -100
		FROM = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_failed_to_protect_me
				who = ROOT
				years = 20
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				letter_event = { id = empire_wars.17 }
			}
		}
		any_realm_lord = {
			limit = { NOT = { character = FROM } }
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_failed_to_protect_vassal
				who = ROOT
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}
}
