#Crown Loyalist joins King
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.19
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.19"
	picture = GFX_evt_empirewar

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		#has_global_flag = empire_civil_war
		# OR = {
			# tier = DUKE
			# tier = COUNT
		# }
		war = no
		OR = {
			is_patrician = no #dont break republic
			is_merchant_republic = yes
		}
		is_nomadic = no
		# OR = { #Republics are not split from Merchant Republics
			# liege = { character = ROOT }
			# liege = { is_merchant_republic = no }
			# is_republic = no
			# tier = COUNT
			# capital_scope = { NOT = { port = yes } }
		# }
		FROMFROM = {
			war = yes
		}
		OR = {
			tier = KING
			NOT = { top_liege = { character = ROOT } }
		}
		OR = {
			has_character_flag = inherit_war
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = supporting_king
					has_character_flag = neutral
					has_character_flag = against_king
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					primary_title = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } } } #independent
					NOT = { #Make sure isnt actually part of another empire
						any_independent_ruler = {
							tier = EMPEROR
							NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
							any_demesne_title = {
								tier = EMPEROR
								ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
								check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FROMFROM = {
				set_empire_war_empire_variable_ROOT_effect = yes
			}
		}
		#Temp workaround for vanilla wrong 'fired from council' opinion bug
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = not_fired_from_council }
			remove_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_fired_from_council }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.19"
		clr_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist
		set_character_flag = supporting_king
		clr_character_flag = neutral
		clr_character_flag = against_king
		clr_character_flag = inherit_war
		clr_character_flag = empire_war_remove_leader
		if = {
			limit = { tier = KING }
			hidden_tooltip = { set_defacto_liege = ROOT }
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_primary_war_defender = yes
						any_war = {
							attacker = { trait = rebel_leader }
							defender = { character = PREVPREV }
						}
					}
					ROOT = { join_defender_wars = PREV }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_primary_war_attacker = yes
						any_war = {
							defender = { trait = rebel_leader }
							attacker = { character = PREVPREV }
						}
					}
					ROOT = { join_attacker_wars = PREV }
				}
				hidden_tooltip = { #failsafe
					ROOT = {
						join_defender_wars = PREV
						join_attacker_wars = PREV
						if = { #If failed, break and add a cooldown
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									any_war = {
										OR = {
											attacker = { character = ROOT_FROM }
											defender = { character = ROOT_FROM }
										}
									}
								}
							}
							clr_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
							set_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
							break = yes
						}
					}
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_loyal_to_crown
					who = ROOT
					years = 10
				}
				hidden_tooltip = {
					letter_event = { id = empire_wars.34 }
					reverse_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_king
						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}
					if = { #Chance of dynastic loyalty
						limit = {
							reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 25 }
							dynasty_head = { character = PREV }
							ROOT = { is_ruler = yes }
						}
						save_event_target_as = potential_loyalty_target
						event_target:new_rebel_leader = { save_event_target_as = potential_loyalty_targets_enemy }
						ROOT = { character_event = { id = dynastic_loyalty.1 days = 4 } }
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				any_vassal = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { war_with = root }
						war = no
						primary_title = {
							mercenary = no
							holy_order = no
						}
						NOT = { tier = BARON }
					}
					clr_character_flag = supporting_king
					clr_character_flag = neutral
					clr_character_flag = against_king
					# clr_character_flag = rebel_leader
					# clr_character_flag = post_civil_war_wars
					# clr_character_flag = independant
					# clr_character_flag = join_independance_asked
					# clr_character_flag = inherit_war
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist }
							NOT = { in_faction = faction_liege_loyalist }
						}
						letter_event = { id = empire_wars.25 days=3 }
					}
					if = { #Crown Loyalists
						limit = { has_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist }
						character_event = { id = empire_wars.19 days=3 }
					}
					if = { #Liege Loyalists
						limit = { in_faction = faction_liege_loyalist }
						character_event = { id = empire_wars.20 days=3 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tier = KING }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { liege = { has_character_flag = against_king NOT = { trait = civil_war } } }
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIP_liege_against_king }
				liege = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						character_event = { id = empire_wars.36 }
					}
					opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_traitor }
				}
				set_character_flag = against_rebel_liege
			}
			if = {
				limit = { liege = { has_character_flag = neutral } }
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIP_liege_neutral }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { liege = { has_character_flag = supporting_king } }
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIP_liege_supporting_king }
				liege = {
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_loyal_to_liege
						who = ROOT
						years = 5
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { liege = { character = FROM } }
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIP_liege_emperor }
				liege = {
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_loyal_to_liege
						who = ROOT
						years = 5
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { liege = { trait = rebel_leader NOT = { trait = civil_war } } }
				custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIP_liege_rebel_leader }
				liege = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						character_event = { id = empire_wars.36 }
					}
					opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_traitor }
				}
				set_character_flag = against_rebel_liege
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						liege = {
							NOT = { has_character_flag = supporting_king }
							NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
						}
						has_character_flag = event_triggered_from_rebel_leader
					}
				}
				liege = {
					if = {
						limit = { higher_tier_than = DUKE }
						hidden_tooltip = { set_empire_war_kingdom_variable_ROOT_effect = yes }
					}
				}
				hidden_tooltip = {
					opinion = { who = liege modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege years = 25 }
					set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				}
				FROM = {
					FROM = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_primary_war_defender = yes
								any_war = {
									attacker = { trait = rebel_leader }
									defender = { character = PREVPREV }
								}
							}
							ROOT = { join_defender_wars = PREV }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_primary_war_attacker = yes
								any_war = {
									defender = { trait = rebel_leader }
									attacker = { character = PREVPREV }
								}
							}
							ROOT = { join_attacker_wars = PREV }
						}
						hidden_tooltip = { #failsafe
							ROOT = {
								join_defender_wars = PREV
								join_attacker_wars = PREV
								if = { #If failed, break and add a cooldown
									limit = {
										NOT = {
											any_war = {
												OR = {
													attacker = { character = ROOT_FROMFROM }
													defender = { character = ROOT_FROMFROM }
												}
											}
										}
									}
									clr_character_flag = event_triggered_from_rebel_leader
									clr_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
									set_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
									break = yes
								}
							}
						}
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_loyal_to_crown
							who = ROOT
							years = 10
						}
						hidden_tooltip = {
							reverse_opinion = {
								modifier = opinion_with_king
								who = ROOT
								years = 100
							}
							letter_event = { id = empire_wars.34 }
							if = { #Chance of dynastic loyalty
								limit = {
									reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 25 }
									dynasty_head = { character = PREV }
									ROOT = { is_ruler = yes }
								}
								save_event_target_as = potential_loyalty_target
								event_target:new_rebel_leader = { save_event_target_as = potential_loyalty_targets_enemy }
								ROOT = { character_event = { id = dynastic_loyalty.1 days = 4 } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = event_triggered_from_rebel_leader
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = { #opinion malus with all opponents
				limit = { independent = yes }
				FROMFROM = {
					any_war = {
						limit = {
							defender = { character = ROOT_FROMFROM }
						}
						any_attacker = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy } }
								NOT = { character = ROOT_FROMFROM }
							}
							opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
							reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
						}
					}
					any_war = {
						limit = {
							attacker = { character = ROOT_FROMFROM }
						}
						any_defender = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy } }
								NOT = { character = ROOT_FROMFROM }
							}
							opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
							reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.20
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.20"
	picture = GFX_evt_empirewar

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		#has_global_flag = empire_civil_war
		OR = {
			tier = DUKE
			tier = COUNT
		}
		war = no
		OR = {
			is_patrician = no #dont break republic
			is_merchant_republic = yes
		}
		is_nomadic = no
		# OR = { #Republics are not split from Merchant Republics
			# liege = { character = ROOT }
			# liege = { is_merchant_republic = no }
			# is_republic = no
			# tier = COUNT
			# capital_scope = { NOT = { port = yes } }
		# }
		FROMFROM = {
			war = yes
		}
		#OR = {
			#tier = KING
			NOT = { top_liege = { character = ROOT } }
		#}
		OR = {
			has_character_flag = inherit_war
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = supporting_king
					has_character_flag = neutral
					has_character_flag = against_king
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.20"
		clr_character_flag = event_triggered_from_rebel_leader
		clr_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist
		clr_character_flag = empire_war_remove_leader
		if = {
			limit = { liege = { has_character_flag = against_king } }
			custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIP_liege_against_king }
			liege = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_loyal_to_liege
					who = ROOT
					years = 5
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = supporting_king
			clr_character_flag = neutral
			set_character_flag = against_king
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = { #Chance of dynastic loyalty
					limit = {
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 25 }
						dynasty_head = { character = PREV }
						ROOT = { is_ruler = yes }
					}
					save_event_target_as = potential_loyalty_target
					FROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = potential_loyalty_targets_enemy }
					ROOT = { character_event = { id = dynastic_loyalty.1 days = 4 } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { liege = { has_character_flag = neutral } }
			custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIP_liege_neutral }
			liege = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_loyal_to_liege
					who = ROOT
					years = 5
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = supporting_king
			set_character_flag = neutral
			clr_character_flag = against_king
		}
		if = {
			limit = { liege = { has_character_flag = supporting_king } }
			custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIP_liege_supporting_king }
			liege = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_loyal_to_liege
					who = ROOT
					years = 5
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = supporting_king
			clr_character_flag = neutral
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = { #Chance of dynastic loyalty
					limit = {
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 25 }
						dynasty_head = { character = PREV }
						ROOT = { is_ruler = yes }
					}
					save_event_target_as = potential_loyalty_target
					event_target:new_rebel_leader = { save_event_target_as = potential_loyalty_targets_enemy }
					ROOT = { character_event = { id = dynastic_loyalty.1 days = 4 } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { liege = { trait = civil_war } }
			custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIP_liege_emperor }
			liege = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_loyal_to_liege
					who = ROOT
					years = 5
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = supporting_king
			clr_character_flag = neutral
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = { #Chance of dynastic loyalty
					limit = {
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 25 }
						dynasty_head = { character = PREV }
						ROOT = { is_ruler = yes }
					}
					save_event_target_as = potential_loyalty_target
					event_target:new_rebel_leader = { save_event_target_as = potential_loyalty_targets_enemy }
					ROOT = { character_event = { id = dynastic_loyalty.1 days = 4 } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { liege = { trait = rebel_leader } }
			custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIP_liege_rebel_leader  }
			liege = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_loyal_to_liege
					who = ROOT
					years = 5

			}
			clr_character_flag = supporting_king

					}

					ROOT = { character_event = { id = dynastic_loyalty.1 days = 4 } }
				}
			}
		}

#Vassal control events
#-----------------------

#AI vassal yearly pulse
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.21

	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	only_playable = yes
	ai = yes

	trigger = {
		demesne_size = 1
		OR = {
			is_patrician = no #dont break republic
			is_merchant_republic = yes
		}
		is_nomadic = no
		OR = {
			independent = no
			primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } }
		}
		OR = {
			had_character_flag = { flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown days = 150 }
			NOT = { has_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown }
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = flag_crown_loyalist }
		NOT = { in_faction = faction_liege_loyalist }
		OR = { #High Septon must have enough authority
			NOT = { has_landed_title = k_cult_of_sigmar }
			crownlaw_title = {
				OR = {
					has_law = investiture_law_2
					has_law = investiture_law_3
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			AND = { #Conditions for Elector Counts
				tier = KING
				OR = {
					AND = {
						war = no #Cannot already of chosen sides
						independent = yes
					}
					liege = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						war = yes
						primary_title = {
							check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
							NOT = { has_title_flag = indep_war }
						}
					}
				}
				NAND = { #If already flagged as supporting king cannot choose sides (will be added back to war automatically)
					has_character_flag = supporting_king
					civil_war = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						war = yes
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_with_king }
						primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 } }
					}
				}
			}
			AND = { #Conditions for vassals Elector Counts
				#ai = no #temp
				lower_tier_than = KING
				NOT = { #Cannot be involved in a non-empire war
					any_war = {
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								attacker = { tier = EMPEROR trait = civil_war }
								defender = { tier = EMPEROR trait = civil_war }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = { #Cannot already have defected
					NOT = { independent = yes }
					war = no
				}
				OR = { #Initial choice event must have occured
					has_character_flag = supporting_king
					has_character_flag = neutral
					has_character_flag = against_king
				}
				OR = {
					independent = yes #Is neutral
					liege = {
						NOT = { has_character_flag = inherit_war } #Liege must not be deciding after inheriting
						OR = { #Liege must be part of the Empire
							NOT = { has_character_flag = independant }
							AND = {
								tier = EMPEROR
								trait = civil_war
							}
						}
						OR = { #Liege must have decided their stance
							AND = {
								tier = EMPEROR
								trait = civil_war
							}
							has_character_flag = supporting_king
							has_character_flag = neutral
							has_character_flag = against_king
							trait = rebel_leader
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		capital_holding = { controller = { character = ROOT } } #Cannot change sides if capital is occupied
		NOT = { #not split when outside force is claiming title
			any_realm_title = {
				any_war = {
					attacker = {
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
				}
				#holder_scope = { war = yes }
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		#find rebel leader
		clr_character_flag = inherit_war
		rebel_leader = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
				is_ruler = yes
				civil_war = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					war_with = PREV
					OR = {
						is_vassal_or_below = ROOT
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = EMPEROR
							ROOT = {
								primary_title = {
									is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 } }
					NAND = { #not enemy rebels
						ROOT = { has_character_flag = supporting_king }
						OR = {
							current_heir = { character = ROOT }
							PREV = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_vengeance } }
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = { #Vassal of rebel leader cannot defect to other rebel leaders
					OR = {
						independent = yes
						liege = {
							OR = { #Vassal of rebel leader cannot defect to other rebel leaders
								NOT = { trait = rebel_leader }
								trait = civil_war
								character = PREVPREV
							}
						}
					}
				}

				NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_deciding_rebel_leader } }
			}
			reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_deciding_rebel_leader months = 1 }
			character_event = { id = empire_wars.2190 } #set rebel leader as FROMFROM scope

			#If other potential rebel leader available repeat event
			if = {
				limit = {
					rebel_leader = {
						is_alive = yes
						is_ruler = yes
						NOT = { character = PREV }
						civil_war = {
							tier = EMPEROR
							war_with = PREV
							OR = {
								is_vassal_or_below = ROOT
								any_demesne_title = {
									tier = EMPEROR
									ROOT = {
										primary_title = {
											is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }
										}
									}
								}
							}
							NAND = { #not enemy rebels
								ROOT = { has_character_flag = supporting_king }
								OR = {
									current_heir = { character = ROOT }
									PREV = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_vengeance } }
								}
							}
							primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 } }
						}
						NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_deciding_rebel_leader } }
					}
				}
				ROOT = { character_event = { id = empire_wars.21 days = 2 } }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}

					is_vassal_or_below = FROM
					any_demesne_title = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						FROM = {
							primary_title = {
								is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }
							}
						}
						check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
					}
				}

#Set emperor as FROM scope
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.22
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		FROM = { #check for erroneous civil_war trait
			if = {
				limit = {
					trait = civil_war
					NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
				}
				remove_trait = civil_war
			}
		}
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { tier = KING }
				character_event = { id = empire_wars.24 }
				break = yes
			}
			#Lower tier than king
			character_event = { id = empire_wars.26 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
#On death vassal inherit control, set FROM scope to relevent emperor
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.23
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.23"

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	immediate = { #find rebel leader
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = against_king  }
			event_target:inherited_rebel_leader = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						trait = rebel_leader
						is_alive = yes
						is_ruler = yes
					}
					character_event = { id = empire_wars.2190 } #set rebel leader as FROMFROM scope
					break = yes
				}
			}
		}
		rebel_leader = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
				is_ruler = yes
				civil_war = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					war_with = PREV
					OR = {
						is_vassal_or_below = ROOT
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = EMPEROR
							ROOT = {
								primary_title = {
									is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 } }
				}
				ROOT = { #Vassal of rebel leader cannot defect to other rebel leaders
					OR = {
						independent = yes
						liege = {
							OR = { #Vassal of rebel leader cannot defect to other rebel leaders
								NOT = { trait = rebel_leader }
								trait = civil_war
								character = PREVPREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_deciding_rebel_leader months = 1 }
			character_event = { id = empire_wars.2190 } #set rebel leader as FROMFROM scope
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
#King/Elector Count tier character decides, FROM is emperor, FROMFROM is rebel leader
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.24
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.24"
	picture = GFX_evt_empirewar

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		#has_global_flag = empire_civil_war
		tier = KING
		is_nomadic = no
		FROM = { war = yes }
		OR = {
			NOT = { war_with = FROM }
			has_character_flag = inherit_war
		}
		OR = {
			independent = yes
			liege = { character = FROM }
		}
		FROM = { primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 } } }
	}

			###Set Empire Title Law 'Flag'###
			clr_character_flag = independant
			FROM = {
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege years = 25 }
				set_empire_war_empire_variable_ROOT_effect = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { independent = no }
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #If granted Elector Count reset Empire war flags
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_granted_kingdom
					}
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			clr_character_flag = neutral
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTEempire_wars.7" #Regent, can choose not to fracture from realm
		trigger = {
				FROM = {
					has_regent = yes
					regent = { character = ROOT }
				}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 500
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				has_character_flag = supporting_king
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = against_king
				trait = honorable
			}
			remove_trait = honorable
		}
		set_character_flag = supporting_king
		clr_character_flag = neutral
		clr_character_flag = against_king
		clr_character_flag = inherit_war
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = TOOLTIPEVTOPTEempire_wars.7
		}
		FROM = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_loyal_to_crown
				who = ROOT
				years = 10
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				reverse_opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_with_king
					who = ROOT
					years = 100
				}
				letter_event = { id = empire_wars.34 }
			}
		}
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_allied_with = ROOT
						has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = broke_alliance
					who = ROOT
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_dynasty_loyalist }
					NOT = { dynasty = ROOT_FROM }
				}
				ROOT = {
					change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = maintenance.3 } }#dishonour trait
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = { NOT = { tier = BARON } }
				set_character_flag = supporting_king
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				clr_character_flag = against_king
			}
			FROM = { #opinion malus with all opponents
				any_war = {
					limit = {
						defender = { character = ROOT_FROM }
					}
					any_attacker = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy } }
							NOT = { character = ROOT_FROM }
						}
						opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
					}
				}
				any_war = {
					limit = {
						attacker = { character = ROOT_FROM }
					}
					any_defender = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy } }
							NOT = { character = ROOT_FROM }
						}
						opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.7" #support the king

			}

				has_character_flag = inherit_war
				has_character_flag = against_king
			}
		}

			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				has_character_flag = supporting_king

				trait = ambitious
				has_character_flag = against_king
			}
			modifier = { #Don't want to support foreign pretender
				factor = 5
				FROM = {
					religion = ROOT
					culture_group = ROOT
					any_demesne_title = { #One of the empire tier titles is being contested
						tier = EMPEROR
						any_war = {

								character = ROOT_FROMFROM
								OR = {

									NOT = { culture_group = ROOT }

							}
							NOT = {
								OR = {
									using_cb = bid_for_independence
									using_cb = cb_faction_independence
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Never join if like rebel and have no relation to king
				factor = 0
				NOT = { is_allied_with = FROM }
				NOT = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = FROM }
				NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_dynasty_loyalist } }
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = 50 } }
				NOT = { is_close_relative = FROM }
				NOT = { is_married = FROM }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = supporting_king }
				FROMFROM = {

					OR = {

						has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						is_married = ROOT

		clr_character_flag = inherit_war
		hidden_tooltip = {

				limit = { independent = no }
				set_defacto_liege = THIS
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_primary_war_defender = yes
					any_war = {
						attacker = { character = ROOT_FROMFROM }
						defender = { character = PREVPREV }
					}
				}
				ROOT = { join_defender_wars = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_primary_war_attacker = yes
					any_war = {
						defender = { character = ROOT_FROMFROM }
						attacker = { character = PREVPREV }
					}
				}
				ROOT = { join_attacker_wars = PREV }
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { #failsafe
				ROOT = {
					join_defender_wars = PREV
					join_attacker_wars = PREV
					if = { #If failed, break and add a cooldown
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								any_war = {
									OR = {
										attacker = { character = ROOT_FROM }
										defender = { character = ROOT_FROM }
									}
								}
							}
						}
						clr_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
						set_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
						break = yes
					}
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_loyal_to_crown
				who = ROOT
				years = 10
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {

					}
					any_attacker = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy } }

						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }

#Vassal of Elector Count/King initial response
letter_event = {
	id = empire_wars.25
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.25"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		#has_global_flag = empire_civil_war
		OR = {
			tier = DUKE
			tier = COUNT
		}
		war = no
		OR = {
			is_patrician = no #dont break republic
			is_merchant_republic = yes
		}
		is_nomadic = no
		FROMFROM = {
			war = yes
		}
		NOT = { top_liege = { character = ROOT } }
		OR = {
			has_character_flag = inherit_war
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = supporting_king
					has_character_flag = neutral
					has_character_flag = against_king
				}
			}
		}
		OR = { #Cannot change sides if capital is occupied
			independent = yes
			is_ruler = no
			capital_holding = { controller = { character = ROOT } }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
		###Set Empire Title Law 'Flag'###
		clr_character_flag = independant
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = yes
				OR = {
					primary_title = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } } } #independent
					NOT = { #Make sure isnt actually part of another empire
						any_independent_ruler = {
							tier = EMPEROR
							NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
							any_demesne_title = {
								tier = EMPEROR
								check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
								ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FROMFROM = {
				if = {
					limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
					set_empire_war_empire_variable_ROOT_effect = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { independent = no }
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #Check Elector Count Status
			limit = { FROM = { FROM = { has_landed_title = e_the_empire } }	}
			if = { #Elector Count
				limit = {
					has_landed_title = k_reikland
					event_target:new_rebel_leader = {
						NOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } } } #The Empire
						NOT = { liege_before_war = { character = FROMFROM } }
						any_war = { defender = { character = FROMFROM } }
					}
				}
				set_character_flag = elector_called_to_arms
			}
		}
	}

							}
						}

			limit = { liege = { has_character_flag = neutral } }
			custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIP_liege_neutral }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { liege = { trait = civil_war } }
			custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIP_liege_emperor }
			set_character_flag = against_loyal_liege
			liege = {
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = { id = empire_wars.36 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { liege = { trait = civil_war } }
				OR = {
					liege = { trait = rebel_leader }
					liege = { character = event_target:new_rebel_leader }
					has_character_flag = event_triggered_from_rebel_leader
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIP_liege_rebel_leader  }
			liege = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_loyal_to_liege
					who = ROOT
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { liege = { has_character_flag = against_king } }
			custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIP_liege_against_king }
			liege = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_loyal_to_liege
					who = ROOT
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = elector_called_to_arms	}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = TOOLTIPELECTOREMPIREWARWARNING
				hidden_tooltip = {
					any_playable_ruler = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_liege_or_above = ROOT
								is_liege_or_above = FROMFROM
								primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } } #The Empire
							}
						}
						opinion = { modifier = opinion_bad_elector who = ROOT years = 10 }
					}
				}
			}
			prestige = -400
			FROMFROM = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_elector_no_defend
					who = ROOT
					years = 10
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = elector_called_to_arms
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_character_flag = event_triggered_from_rebel_leader }
				NOT = {
					liege = {
						OR = {
							has_character_flag = against_king
							character = event_target:new_rebel_leader
							trait = rebel_leader
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_ruler = yes }
				liege = {
					if = {
						limit = { higher_tier_than = DUKE }
						hidden_tooltip = { set_empire_war_kingdom_variable_ROOT_effect = yes }
					}
				}
				set_character_flag = empire_war_remove_leader
				hidden_tooltip = {
					liege = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege years = 25 } }
					set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				}
				event_target:new_rebel_leader = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_primary_war_defender = yes
							any_war = {
								attacker = { character = FROMFROM }
								defender = { character = PREVPREV }
							}
						}
						ROOT = { join_defender_wars = PREV }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_primary_war_attacker = yes
							any_war = {
								defender = { character = FROMFROM }
								attacker = { character = PREVPREV }
							}
						}
						ROOT = { join_attacker_wars = PREV }
					}
					hidden_tooltip = { #failsafe
						ROOT = {
							join_defender_wars = PREV
							join_attacker_wars = PREV
							if = { #If failed, break and add a cooldown
								limit = {
									NOT = {
										any_war = {
											OR = {
												attacker = { character = event_target:new_rebel_leader }
												defender = { character = event_target:new_rebel_leader }
											}
										}
									}
								}
								clr_character_flag = event_triggered_from_rebel_leader
								clr_character_flag = empire_war_remove_leader
								clr_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
								set_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
								break = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:new_rebel_leader = {
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					who = ROOT
					years = 10
				}
				hidden_tooltip = {
					letter_event = { id = empire_wars.30 }
					reverse_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}
					if = { #Chance of dynastic loyalty
						limit = {
							reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 25 }
							dynasty_head = { character = PREV }
							ROOT = { is_ruler = yes }
						}
						save_event_target_as = potential_loyalty_target
						ROOT_FROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = potential_loyalty_targets_enemy }
						ROOT = { character_event = { id = dynastic_loyalty.1 days = 4 } }
					}
				}
			}
			FROMFROM = {
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = { id = empire_wars.32 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ruler = no }
			FROMFROM = { opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_traitor } }
		}
		set_character_flag = against_king
		clr_character_flag = neutral
		clr_character_flag = supporting_king
		clr_character_flag = event_triggered_from_rebel_leader
		clr_character_flag = empire_war_remove_leader
		FROM = {
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_allied_with = ROOT
							has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					opinion = {
						modifier = broke_alliance
						who = ROOT
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_dynasty_loyalist }
						NOT = { dynasty = ROOT_FROM }
					}
					ROOT = {
						change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 }
						hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = maintenance.3 } }#dishonour trait
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = { #opinion malus with all opponents
				limit = { independent = yes }
				FROMFROM = { #opinion malus with all opponents
					any_war = {
						limit = {
							defender = { character = ROOT_FROMFROM }
						}
						any_defender = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy } }
								NOT = { character = ROOT_FROMFROM }
							}
							opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
							reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
						}
					}
					any_war = {
						limit = {
							attacker = { character = ROOT_FROMFROM }
						}
						any_attacker = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy } }
								NOT = { character = ROOT_FROMFROM }
							}
							opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
							reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTempire_warsTOOLTIP"
		trigger = { ai = no }
		custom_tooltip = { text = EVTTOOLTIPempire_warsTOOLTIP }
		hidden_tooltip = { repeat_event = { id = empire_wars.25 } }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			#Temp workaround for vanilla wrong 'fired from council' opinion bug
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_modifier = not_fired_from_council }
				remove_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_fired_from_council }
			}
		}
	}
}
#Vassal of Elector Count/King  inherit/yearly decision FROM is emperor, FROMFROM is rebel leader
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.26
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.26"
	picture = GFX_evt_empirewar

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		#has_global_flag = empire_civil_war
		OR = {
			tier = DUKE
			tier = COUNT
		}
		OR = {
			is_patrician = no #dont break republic
			is_merchant_republic = yes
		}
		is_nomadic = no
		FROM = { war = yes }
		OR = {
			NOT = { liege = { character = ROOT } }
			NOT = { war_with = FROM }
			has_character_flag = inherit_war
		}
		FROM = { primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 } } }
		NAND = { #Landless dragon riders must have an interest in getting involved
			trait = dragon_rider
			is_ruler = no
			liege = { #will always consider if liege is a belligerent or hated
				NOR = {
					character = FROM
					trait = rebel_leader
					NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = -50 } }
				}
			}
			OR = { #Reasons to stay
				AND = { #On council and like liege
					is_councillor = yes
					liege = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 } }
				}
				liege = { #Liege is relative or loved
					OR = {
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						dynasty = ROOT
						reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 50 }
					}
				}
				AND = { #Foreign war
					liege = { culture_group = ROOT }
					NOT = { culture_group = FROM }
					NOT = { culture_group = FROMFROM }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		###Set Empire Title Law 'Flag'###
		clr_character_flag = independant
		#Check which rebel leader is with
		clear_event_target = actual_rebel_leader
		clear_event_target = current_rebel_leader
		FROMFROM = { save_event_target_as = actual_rebel_leader } #for AI logic, actual rebel leader may be changed below
		liege = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					NOT = { trait = civil_war }
					NOT = { trait = rebel_leader }
					has_character_flag = against_king
					NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROMFROM modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader } }
				}
				rebel_leader = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = PREV modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader }
					}
					save_event_target_as = current_rebel_leader
					save_event_target_as = actual_rebel_leader
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
					NOT = { character = FROMFROM }
					NOT = { trait = civil_war }
					trait = rebel_leader
					war_with = FROM
				}
				save_event_target_as = current_rebel_leader
				save_event_target_as = actual_rebel_leader
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					primary_title = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } } } #independent
					NOT = { #Make sure isnt actually part of another empire
						any_independent_ruler = {
							tier = EMPEROR
							NOT = { character = FROM }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
							any_demesne_title = {
								tier = EMPEROR
								check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
								ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				set_empire_war_empire_variable_ROOT_effect = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { independent = no }
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {

							defender = { character = PREVPREV }
							attacker = { character = event_target:current_rebel_leader }
							war_score = 80
						}
					}
				}
			}
			###########
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				any_dynasty_member = {
					is_close_relative = ROOT
					host = { character = event_target:current_rebel_leader }
				}
			}
			modifier = { #close family
				factor = 5
				OR = {
					is_child_of = event_target:current_rebel_leader
					is_married = event_target:current_rebel_leader
					any_child = { character = event_target:current_rebel_leader }
					any_child = { any_child = { character = event_target:current_rebel_leader } }
				}
			}
			modifier = { #alliance
				factor = 4
				OR = {
					is_allied_with = event_target:current_rebel_leader
					has_non_aggression_pact_with = event_target:current_rebel_leader
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				has_opinion_modifier = { who = event_target:current_rebel_leader modifier = opinion_dynasty_loyalist }
			}
			#allied with ally of king
			modifier = { #alliance
				factor = 2.5
				any_allied_character = {
					war_with = FROM
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.35
				culture_group = event_target:current_rebel_leader
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.35
				religion = event_target:current_rebel_leader
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				NOT = { trait = dragon_rider }
				event_target:current_rebel_leader = {
					trait = dragon_rider
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				event_target:current_rebel_leader = {
					trait = lunatic
					ROOT = {
						NOT = { trait = lunatic }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 6
				is_rival = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 6
				is_friend = event_target:current_rebel_leader
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				is_friend = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				is_rival = event_target:current_rebel_leader
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				opinion = { who = event_target:current_rebel_leader value =  20 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				opinion = { who = event_target:current_rebel_leader value =  40 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				opinion = { who = event_target:current_rebel_leader value =  60 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				opinion = { who = event_target:current_rebel_leader value =  80 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				opinion = { who = event_target:current_rebel_leader value =  100 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = event_target:current_rebel_leader value = 0 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = event_target:current_rebel_leader value = -20 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = event_target:current_rebel_leader value = -40 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = event_target:current_rebel_leader value = -60 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { opinion = { who = event_target:current_rebel_leader value = -80 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.7
				NOT = { opinion = { who = event_target:current_rebel_leader value = -99 } }
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					has_character_flag = against_king
					reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value =  20 }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					has_character_flag = against_king
					reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value =  40 }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					has_character_flag = against_king
					reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value =  60 }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					has_character_flag = against_king
					reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value =  80 }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					has_character_flag = against_king
					reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value =  100 }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					has_character_flag = against_king
					NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value =  0 } }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					has_character_flag = against_king
					reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value =  -20 }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					has_character_flag = against_king
					reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value =  -40 }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					has_character_flag = against_king
					reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value =  -60 }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					has_character_flag = against_king
				}
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					has_character_flag = against_king
				}
				trait = content
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				event_target:current_rebel_leader = {
					NOT = { is_vassal_or_below = ROOT }
					any_war = {
							using_cb = bid_for_independence
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Never join if like king and have no relation to rebel
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					opinion = { who = FROM value = 50 }
					is_close_relative = FROM
					is_married = FROM
				}
				event_target:current_rebel_leader = {
					NOT = { is_vassal_or_below = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_allied_with = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT }
					NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 50 } }
					NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_married = ROOT }
					NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader } }
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Foreign invader reluctance
				factor = 0
				culture_group = FROM
				opinion = { who = FROM value = -30 }
				event_target:current_rebel_leader = {
					NOT = { is_vassal_or_below = ROOT }
					NOT = { culture_group = ROOT }
					NOT = { primary_title = { ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } } } }
					NOT = { has_character_flag = claimant_adventurer }

					NOT = { is_allied_with = ROOT }
					NOT = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT }
					NOT = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT value = 50 } }
					NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_married = ROOT }
					NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { trait = civil_war }
					trait = rebel_leader
					character = event_target:current_rebel_leader
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIP_liege_rebel_leader  }
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = inherit_war }
				liege = {
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_loyal_to_liege
						who = ROOT
						years = 5
					}
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = against_rebel_liege
			clr_character_flag = against_loyal_liege
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					has_character_flag = against_king
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIP_liege_against_king }
			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = inherit_war }
				liege = {
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_loyal_to_liege
						who = ROOT
						years = 5
					}
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = against_rebel_liege
			clr_character_flag = against_loyal_liege
		}
		set_character_flag = against_king
		clr_character_flag = neutral
		clr_character_flag = supporting_king
		clr_character_flag = event_triggered_from_rebel_leader
		clr_character_flag = empire_war_remove_leader
		clr_character_flag = inherit_war
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_allied_with = ROOT
						has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = broke_alliance
					who = ROOT
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_dynasty_loyalist }
					NOT = { dynasty = event_target:current_rebel_leader }
				}
				ROOT = {
					change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = maintenance.3 } }#dishonour trait
				}
			}
		}
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_allied_with = ROOT
						has_non_aggression_pact_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				opinion = {
					modifier = broke_alliance
					who = ROOT
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_dynasty_loyalist }
					NOT = { dynasty = event_target:current_rebel_leader }
				}
				ROOT = {
					change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = maintenance.3 } }#dishonour trait
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = { #opinion malus with all opponents
				limit = { independent = yes }
				FROM = {
					any_war = {
						limit = {
							defender = { character = ROOT_FROM }
						}
						any_defender = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy } }
								NOT = { character = ROOT_FROM }
							}
							opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
							reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
						}
					}
					any_war = {
						limit = {
							attacker = { character = ROOT_FROM }
						}
						any_attacker = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy } }
								NOT = { character = ROOT_FROM }
							}
							opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
							reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_civil_war_enemy }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Inform rebel of partner (from war start)
letter_event = {
	id = empire_wars.30
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.30"

	is_triggered_only = yes
	ai = no

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = empire_war_small_lord_i_dont_care }
			FROM = { higher_tier_than = DUKE }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.30" #Yes
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAEMPIREWARIDONTCARE" #Yes
		trigger = {
			FROM = { NOT = { higher_tier_than = DUKE } }
		}
		set_character_flag = empire_war_small_lord_i_dont_care
	}
}

#Flag maintenance
#----------------------
#Call to arms accepted set flags
letter_event = {
	id = empire_wars.41

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				tier = EMPEROR
				trait = civil_war
			}
			trait = rebel_leader
		}
	}

	desc = "EVTDESC238"

	option = {
		name = "OK"
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					trait = civil_war
					FROM = {
						OR = {
							primary_title = {
								ROOT = {
									any_demesne_title = {
										tier = EMPEROR
										is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }
									}
								}
							}
							is_liege_or_above = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					clr_character_flag = inherit_war
					clr_character_flag = neutral
					clr_character_flag = against_king
					set_character_flag = supporting_king
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_king
						who = PREV
						years = 100
					}
				}
				break = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					trait = rebel_leader
					war = yes
					any_current_enemy = { tier = EMPEROR }
					OR = {
						FROM = { primary_title = { ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } } } }
						any_current_enemy = {
							tier = EMPEROR
							primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 } }
							any_demesne_title = {
								tier = EMPEROR
								FROM = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					clr_character_flag = inherit_war
					clr_character_flag = neutral
					clr_character_flag = supporting_king
					set_character_flag = against_king
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = PREV
						years = 100
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
# Maintain defacto opinion link with split vassal
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.42
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.42"

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes  ###FLAG### temp for testing
	only_independent = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
		NOT = { culture_group = unoccupied_group }
		primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } }
	}

	immediate = {
		random_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				tier = EMPEROR
				any_demesne_title = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
					check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
				}
				NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_granted_independence } }
			}
			reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege years = 25 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 1 } } }
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					higher_tier_than = DUKE
					higher_tier_than = ROOT
					any_demesne_title = {
						higher_tier_than = DUKE
						check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0.9 }
						ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" which = PREVPREV } } }
					}
					NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_granted_independence } }
				}
				reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege years = 25 }
			}
		}
		#if still no liege found they must be independent
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_opinion_modifier_target = {
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
						higher_tier_than = DUKE
						higher_tier_than = ROOT
						NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_granted_independence } }
					}
				}
			}
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tier = BARON }
					NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
				}
				set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "OK"
	}
}
#Vassal of split vassal rebels, add defacto liege link to emperor
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.4299

	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	only_independent = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
		FROM = { liege_before_war = { character = ROOT } }
		primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 } }
	}

	immediate = {
		primary_title = {
			FROM = {
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						NOT = { tier = BARON }
					}
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }
				}
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						lower_tier_than = KING
						NOT = { tier = BARON }
					}
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" which = PREVPREV }
				}
			}
		}
		random_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				tier = EMPEROR
				any_demesne_title = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
					check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
				}
				NOT = { character = ROOT }
			}
			reverse_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege years = 25 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 1 } } }
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					higher_tier_than = DUKE
					higher_tier_than = ROOT
					any_demesne_title = {
						higher_tier_than = DUKE
						check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0.9 }
						ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" which = PREVPREV } } }
					}
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
				}
				reverse_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege years = 25 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "OK"
	}
}

#Character wins indep war maintenance
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.50
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.50"
	picture = GFX_evt_powerful_ruler

	trigger = {
		is_ruler = yes
		liege = { character = ROOT }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	#hide_window = yes

	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = supporting_king
		clr_character_flag = neutral
		clr_character_flag = against_king
		clr_character_flag = join_independance_asked
		clr_character_flag = no_kingship
		clr_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
		clr_character_flag = must_decide
		clr_character_flag = post_civil_war_indep_war

		set_character_flag = ai_flag_never_transfer

		if = {
			limit = { war = no }
			clr_character_flag = rebel_leader
			hidden_tooltip = { remove_trait = rebel_leader }
			clr_character_flag = independant
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_demesne_title = {
				clr_title_flag = indep_war
			}
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
					NOT = { tier = BARON }
				}
				set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
			}
			any_realm_lord = {
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						NOT = { tier = BARON }
					}
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
				}
				clr_character_flag = supporting_king
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				clr_character_flag = against_king
			}
			if = {
				limit = { higher_tier_than = DUKE }
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						tier = KING
						is_variable_equal = { which = "lord_paramount_status" value = 1 } #1 = lord paramount, 2 = interregnum
					}
					hidden_tooltip = { set_variable = { which = "lord_paramount_status" value = 0 } }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { government = feudal_government_LP }
					set_government_type = feudal_government
				}
				any_independent_ruler = { #Re-vassalise any lords split via empire-war
					limit = {
						primary_title = {
							ROOT = {
								any_demesne_title = {
									OR = {
										AND = {
											tier = EMPEROR
											check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
											is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }
										}
										AND = {
											higher_tier_than = DUKE
											check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 1 }
											is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" which = PREVPREV }
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
						lower_tier_than = ROOT
						NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_granted_independence } }
					}
					set_defacto_liege = ROOT
					remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }
					any_demesne_title = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { tier = BARON }
							NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
						}
						set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
					}
					clr_character_flag = supporting_king
					clr_character_flag = neutral
					clr_character_flag = against_king
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.34" #Yes
	}
}
#A Lord that wins independance from Elector Count/King during civil chooses
#whether to swear fealty to Emperor (triggered from indep CB in cb_types)
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.51
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.51"
	picture = GFX_evt_war_planning

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.51" #Yes
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		random_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				tier = EMPEROR
				any_demesne_title = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
					check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { war = no }
				ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { war = yes }
				ROOT = {
					set_character_flag = supporting_king
					clr_character_flag = neutral
					clr_character_flag = against_king
					clr_character_flag = inherit_war
					clr_character_flag = empire_war_remove_leader
					clr_character_flag = elector_called_to_arms
				}
				hidden_tooltip = {
					reverse_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_king
						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_primary_war_defender = yes
						any_war = {
							attacker = { trait = rebel_leader }
							defender = { character = PREVPREV }
						}
					}
					ROOT = { join_defender_wars = PREV }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_primary_war_attacker = yes
						any_war = {
							defender = { trait = rebel_leader }
							attacker = { character = PREVPREV }
						}
					}
					ROOT = { join_attacker_wars = PREV }
				}
				hidden_tooltip = { #failsafe
					ROOT = {
						join_defender_wars = PREV
						join_attacker_wars = PREV
						if = { #If failed, break and add a cooldown
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									any_war = {
										OR = {
											attacker = { character = PREVPREVPREV }
											defender = { character = PREVPREVPREV }
										}
									}
								}
							}
							clr_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
							set_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
							break = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBempire_wars.51" #No
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = { NOT = { tier = BARON } NOT = { tier = EMPEROR } }
				set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
		any_demesne_title = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tier = COUNT
					tier = DUKE
				}
			}
			set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAelector_wars.52" #Yes
	}
}
# Indep War Victory Ally Maintenance
character_event = {
	id = elector_wars.53
	desc = "EVTDESCelector_wars.53"
	picture = GFX_evt_powerful_ruler

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FROM = { tier = EMPEROR }
		OR = {
			has_character_flag = against_king
			has_character_flag = neutral
			has_character_flag = supporting_king
			any_liege = { tier = EMPEROR }
		}
		NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						any_realm_province = {
							any_neighbor_province = {
								any_province_lord = {
									OR = {
										character = ROOT
										is_liege_or_above = ROOT
										liege_before_war = { character = ROOT }
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = swear_fealty
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAelector_wars.53" #Swear Fealty to new King
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = swear_fealty
			war = no
		}
		set_defacto_liege = FROM
		clr_character_flag = swear_fealty
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				set_empire_war_empire_variable_ROOT_effect = yes
			}
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tier = COUNT
						tier = DUKE
					}
				}
				set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0 }
			}
			primary_title = {
				ROOT = {
					any_realm_lord = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { tier = BARON }
								NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
							}
							set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREVPREV }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			clr_character_flag = joined_independance_war
			clr_character_flag = post_civil_war_wars
			clr_character_flag = supporting_king
			clr_character_flag = neutral
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			clr_character_flag = rebel_leader
			clr_character_flag = independant
			clr_character_flag = join_independance_asked
			clr_character_flag = no_kingship
			remove_trait = rebel_leader
			clr_character_flag = elector_war_decision_cooldown
			remove_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBelector_wars.53" #Yes
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = swear_fealty
			war = yes
		}
		clr_character_flag = swear_fealty
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				set_empire_war_empire_variable_ROOT_effect = yes
			}
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tier = COUNT
						tier = DUKE
					}
				}
				set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0 }
			}
			primary_title = {
				ROOT = {
					any_realm_lord = {
						any_demesne_title = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { tier = BARON }
								NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
							}
							set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREVPREV }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = post_civil_war_wars
		clr_character_flag = joined_independance_war
		any_war = {
			limit = { 	using_cb = bid_for_independence
						defender = { character = PREV }
			}
			attacker = { set_character_flag = 	post_civil_war_indep_war }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			clr_character_flag = supporting_king
			clr_character_flag = neutral
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			clr_character_flag = rebel_leader
			clr_character_flag = independant
			clr_character_flag = join_independance_asked
			clr_character_flag = no_kingship
			remove_trait = rebel_leader
			clr_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
			remove_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader }

			character_event = { id = interaction.899 days = 3 } #ask liege for help?
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTCempire_wars.53" #Declare Independence
		trigger = { NOT = { has_character_flag = swear_fealty } }
		set_defacto_liege = ROOT
		hidden_tooltip = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = "indep_faction_won"
				duration = 10
			}
			clr_character_flag = joined_independance_war
			clr_character_flag = post_civil_war_wars
			clr_character_flag = supporting_king
			clr_character_flag = neutral
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			clr_character_flag = rebel_leader
			clr_character_flag = independant
			clr_character_flag = join_independance_asked
			clr_character_flag = no_kingship
			remove_trait = rebel_leader
			clr_character_flag = empire_war_decision_cooldown
			remove_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader }

			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = { NOT = { tier = BARON } NOT = { tier = EMPEROR } }
				set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
			}
			any_realm_lord = {
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = { NOT = { tier = BARON } NOT = { tier = EMPEROR } }
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = empire_wars.54
	desc = "AI-Event"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		ai = yes #Humans can swear fealty to who they want
		NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
		NOT = { tier = KING }
		any_playable_ruler = {
			has_character_modifier = indep_faction_won
			higher_tier_than = ROOT
			any_realm_province = {
				any_neighbor_province = {
					any_province_lord = {
						is_liege_or_above = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "OK"
		random_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = indep_faction_won
				higher_tier_than = ROOT
				any_realm_province = {
					any_neighbor_province = {
						any_province_lord = {
							is_liege_or_above = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV }
		}
	}
}

#Empire War Drama
#-----------------------
#My close relative is opposing my host
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.60
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.60"
	picture = GFX_evt_war_planning

	is_triggered_only = yes
	only_playable = yes
	hide_window = yes
	war = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				tier = EMPEROR
				trait = civil_war
			}
			trait = rebel_leader
		}
		any_current_enemy = {
			war_with = ROOT
			OR = {
				independent = yes
				liege_before_war = { character = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		any_courtier = {
			limit = {
				host = { character = ROOT }
				NOR = { #does not apply to direct family
					is_child_of = ROOT
					father_even_if_dead = { is_child_of = ROOT }
					mother_even_if_dead = { is_child_of = ROOT }
					is_parent_of = ROOT
					is_grandparent_of = ROOT
					sibling = ROOT
					is_married = ROOT
				}
				ROOT = {
					any_current_enemy = {
						war_with = ROOT
						OR = {
							independent = yes
							liege_before_war = { character = ROOT }
						}
						NOT = { character = PREVPREV }
						OR = {
							is_child_of = PREVPREV
							any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREV }
							any_child = { any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREVPREV } }
							sibling = PREVPREV
							is_married = PREVPREV
							AND = { #Can target dynasts only if enemy is close relative
								dynasty = PREVPREV
								NOT = { dynasty = 0 }
								ROOT = { NOT = { dynasty = PREVPREVPREV } }
							}
						}
						NAND = { #Ignore half-siblings who are related to ROOT
							sibling = PREVPREV
							NOT = { is_married = PREVPREV }
							PREVPREV = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
							OR = {
								father_even_if_dead = { NOT = { is_father = PREVPREVPREV } }
								mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { is_mother = PREVPREVPREV } }
							}
						}
						NAND = { #Ignore if courtier is same dynasty but NOT same dynasty as enemy
							NOT = { dynasty = PREVPREV }
							ROOT = { dynasty = PREVPREVPREV }
						}
						NAND = { #If ROOT suspects enemy of being a bastard and is related to target, then ignore
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_suspected_bastard }
							NOR = {
								any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREV }
								any_child = { any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREVPREV } }
								is_married = PREVPREV
							}
							PREVPREV = {
								OR = {
									dynasty = ROOT
									is_close_relative = ROOT
								}
								NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_suspected_bastard } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_merciful } }
				NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_supported_claimant } }
				NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_with_king } }
				NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader } }
				NOT = { ROOT = { supported_claimant = { character = PREVPREV } } }
				NOT = { trait = dragon }
				NOT = { character = ROOT }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = captured_in_battle }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = imprisoned_for_relatives_crimes }
				has_pilgrimage_trait_trigger = no
			}
			character_event = { id = empire_wars.6099 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = OK
	}
}
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.6099
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.60"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.60"
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					ai = no
					FROM = { ai = no }
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				any_current_enemy = {
					limit = {
						war_with = ROOT_FROM
						OR = {
							independent = yes
							liege_before_war = { character = ROOT_FROM }
						}
						NOT = { character = PREVPREV }
						OR = {
							is_child_of = PREVPREV
							any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREV }
							any_child = { any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREVPREV } }
							sibling = PREVPREV
							is_married = PREVPREV
							AND = { #Can target dynasts only if enemy is close relative
								dynasty = PREVPREV
								NOT = { dynasty = 0 }
								ROOT_FROM = { NOT = { dynasty = PREVPREVPREV } }
							}
						}
						NAND = { #Ignore half-siblings who are related to ROOT
							sibling = PREVPREV
							NOT = { is_married = PREVPREV }
							PREVPREV = { is_close_relative = ROOT_FROM }
							OR = {
								father_even_if_dead = { NOT = { is_father = PREVPREVPREV } }
								mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { is_mother = PREVPREVPREV } }
							}
						}
						NAND = { #Ignore if courtier is same dynasty but NOT same dynasty as enemy
							NOT = { dynasty = PREVPREV }
							ROOT_FROM = { dynasty = PREVPREVPREV }
						}
						NAND = { #If ROOT suspects enemy of being a bastard and is related to target, then ignore
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT_FROM modifier = opinion_suspected_bastard }
							NOR = {
								any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREV }
								any_child = { any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREVPREV } }
								is_married = PREVPREV
							}
							PREVPREV = {
								OR = {
									dynasty = ROOT_FROM
									is_close_relative = ROOT_FROM
								}
								NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT_FROM modifier = opinion_suspected_bastard } }
							}
						}
					}
					tooltip = { show_portrait = yes }
					save_event_target_as = empire_war_enemy
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = empire_wars.61 days = 1 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIPempire_wars.61" }
		}
	}
}
#I have a close relative of the enemy
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.61
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.61"
	picture = GFX_evt_judged_by_ruler

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.61" #It's not his fault
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = { #More tolerent of ignorant AI
				factor = 3
				NOT = {
					any_current_enemy = {
						OR = {
							is_child_of = FROM
							is_parent_of = FROM
							any_child = { is_parent_of = FROM }
							sibling = FROM
							is_married = FROM
							AND = { #Can target dynasts only if enemy is close relative
								dynasty = FROM
								NOT = { dynasty = 0 }
								NOT = { dynasty = ROOT }
							}
						}
						war_with = ROOT
						OR = {
							ai = no
							AND = {
								has_character_flag = against_king
								ROOT = { tier = EMPEROR trait = civil_war }
							}
							AND = {
								has_character_flag = supporting_king
								ROOT = { trait = rebel_leader }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				dynasty = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_close_relative = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				opinion = { who = FROM value =  25 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				opinion = { who = FROM value =  50 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				opinion = { who = FROM value =  75 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				trait = charitable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = just
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				trait = trusting
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10 #Enemy has your relative
				any_current_enemy = {
					dynasty = FROM
					is_close_relative = FROM
					any_courtier = {
						host = { character = PREVPREV }
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						AND = {
							NOT = { dynasty = 0 }
							dynasty = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_merciful
				who = ROOT
				years = 10
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = { id = empire_wars.62 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { dynasty = FROM } }
			prestige = -40
		}
		if = {
			limit = { dynasty = FROM }
			prestige = -20
		}
		piety = 20
		change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -3 }
		hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = faction_event_new.90 } }
	}

		name = "EVTOPTBempire_wars.61" #Imprison him
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value =  -25 } }
			}

				factor = 2
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value =  -50 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value =  -75 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				trait = diligent
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5

			}
			modifier = {

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = deceitful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				trait = arbitrary
			}
		}
		FROM = {

			if = {
				limit = { prisoner = no }
				imprison = ROOT

					character_event = { id = empire_wars.67 }
				}
			}
		}

#Informed imprisoned
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.67
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.67"
	picture = "GFX_evt_into_the_dungeon"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.67"
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				any_current_enemy = {
					limit = {
						ai = no

						war_with = ROOT_FROM
						OR = {
							independent = yes
							liege_before_war = { character = ROOT_FROM }
						}
						NOT = { character = PREVPREV }
						OR = {
							is_child_of = PREVPREV
							any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREV }
							any_child = { any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREVPREV } }
							sibling = PREVPREV
							is_married = PREVPREV
							AND = { #Can target dynasts only if enemy is close relative
								dynasty = PREVPREV
								NOT = { dynasty = 0 }
								ROOT_FROM = { NOT = { dynasty = PREVPREVPREV } }
							}
						}
						NAND = { #Ignore half-siblings who are related to ROOT
							sibling = PREVPREV
							NOT = { is_married = PREVPREV }
							PREVPREV = { is_close_relative = ROOT_FROM }
							OR = {
								father_even_if_dead = { NOT = { is_father = PREVPREVPREV } }
								mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { is_mother = PREVPREVPREV } }
							}
						}
						NAND = { #Ignore if courtier is same dynasty but NOT same dynasty as enemy
							NOT = { dynasty = PREVPREV }
							ROOT_FROM = { dynasty = PREVPREVPREV }
						}
						NAND = { #If ROOT suspects enemy of being a bastard and is related to target, then ignore
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT_FROM modifier = opinion_suspected_bastard }
							NOR = {
								any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREV }
								any_child = { any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREVPREV } }
								is_married = PREVPREV
							}
							PREVPREV = {
								OR = {
									dynasty = ROOT_FROM
									is_close_relative = ROOT_FROM
								}
								NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT_FROM modifier = opinion_suspected_bastard } }
							}
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = empire_wars.69 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				killer = FROM
			}

	}
