#Informed tortured (also used in prisoner break chain,  event rescue_prisoner.1399)
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.71
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.71"
	picture = "GFX_evt_torture"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { set_character_flag = alive }

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.71"
		if = {
			limit = { is_female = no }
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					add_character_modifier = {
						name = tortured
						duration = 60
					}
				}
				25 = { add_trait_silently_wounded_effect = yes }
				25 = { add_maimed_trait_effect = yes }
				10 = { add_crippled_trait_effect = yes }
				10 = { add_trait = blinded }
				5 = { add_trait = eunuch }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_female = yes }
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					add_character_modifier = {
						name = tortured
						duration = 60
					}
				}
				25 = { add_trait_silently_wounded_effect = yes }
				25 = { add_maimed_trait_effect = yes }
				15 = { add_crippled_trait_effect = yes }
				10 = { add_trait = blinded }
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				any_current_enemy = {
					limit = {
						war_with = ROOT_FROM
						OR = {
							independent = yes
							liege_before_war = { character = ROOT_FROM }
						}
						NOT = { character = PREVPREV }
						OR = {
							is_child_of = PREVPREV
							any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREV }
							any_child = { any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREVPREV } }
							sibling = PREVPREV
							is_married = PREVPREV
							AND = { #Can target dynasts only if enemy is close relative
								dynasty = PREVPREV
								NOT = { dynasty = 0 }
								ROOT_FROM = { NOT = { dynasty = PREVPREVPREV } }
							}
						}
						NAND = { #Ignore half-siblings who are related to ROOT
							sibling = PREVPREV
							NOT = { is_married = PREVPREV }
							PREVPREV = { is_close_relative = ROOT_FROM }
							OR = {
								father_even_if_dead = { NOT = { is_father = PREVPREVPREV } }
								mother_even_if_dead = { NOT = { is_mother = PREVPREVPREV } }
							}
						}
						NAND = { #Ignore if courtier is same dynasty but NOT same dynasty as enemy
							NOT = { dynasty = PREVPREV }
							ROOT_FROM = { dynasty = PREVPREVPREV }
						}
						NAND = { #If ROOT suspects enemy of being a bastard and is related to target, then ignore
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT_FROM modifier = opinion_suspected_bastard }
							NOR = {
								any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREV }
								any_child = { any_child = { character = PREVPREVPREVPREV } }
								is_married = PREVPREV
							}
							PREVPREV = {
								OR = {
									dynasty = ROOT_FROM
									is_close_relative = ROOT_FROM
								}
								NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT_FROM modifier = opinion_suspected_bastard } }
							}
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = empire_wars.72 }
				}
			}
		}
		random = {
			chance = 33
			clr_character_flag = alive
			death = {
				death_reason = death_execution_torture
				killer = FROM
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				FROM = {
					character_event = { id = empire_wars.73 }
					set_character_flag = unjust_execution
					#set_character_flag = special_execution_found
					save_event_target_as = executioner
				}
				character_event = { id = 45342 } #Universal on_execution event
			}
		}
		if = { #If still alive apply 'tortured me' opinion penalty
			limit = { has_character_flag = alive }
			clr_character_flag = alive
			hidden_tooltip = {
				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					modifier = opinion_tortured_me
				}
				mother = {
					set_character_flag = murder_opinion_set
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						modifier = opinion_tortured_kin
					}
				}
				father = {
					set_character_flag = murder_opinion_set
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						modifier = opinion_tortured_kin
					}
				}
				any_child = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_opinion_set }
					}
					set_character_flag = murder_opinion_set
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						modifier = opinion_tortured_kin
					}
				}
				any_spouse = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = -25 }
						NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_opinion_set }
					}
					set_character_flag = murder_opinion_set
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						modifier = opinion_tortured_kin
					}
				}
				any_lover = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_opinion_set }
					}
					set_character_flag = murder_opinion_set
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						modifier = opinion_tortured_lover
					}
				}
				any_friend = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_opinion_set }
					}
					set_character_flag = murder_opinion_set
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						modifier = opinion_tortured_friend
					}
				}
				any_dynasty_member = {
					limit = {
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						NOT = { character = FROM }
						NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_opinion_set }
					}
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						modifier = opinion_tortured_kin
					}
				}
				mother = { clr_character_flag = murder_opinion_set	}
				father = { clr_character_flag = murder_opinion_set }
				any_child = { clr_character_flag = murder_opinion_set }
				any_lover = { clr_character_flag = murder_opinion_set }
				any_friend = { clr_character_flag = murder_opinion_set }
				any_spouse = { clr_character_flag = murder_opinion_set }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Emperor deals with defeated rebels/traitors
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.74
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.74"
	picture = GFX_evt_judged_by_ruler

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		demesne_size = 1
		NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
		FROM = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = civil_war
						ROOT = {
							NOT = { has_character_flag = independant }
							NOT = { any_liege = { has_character_flag = independant } }
						}
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = EMPEROR
							ROOT = {
								primary_title = {
									lower_tier_than = EMPEROR
									is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }
								}
							}
							check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
						}
					}
					ROOT = { liege_before_war = { character = PREVPREV } }
					ROOT = { liege = { character = PREVPREV } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_trait = civil_war }
		FROMFROM = {
			reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege years = 25 }
			set_empire_war_empire_variable_ROOT_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = yes
				lower_tier_than = KING
				primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 1 } }
				NOT = { liege = { character = FROMFROM } }
			}
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					liege = {
						higher_tier_than = DUKE
						any_demesne_title = {
							higher_tier_than = DUKE
							ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" which = PREVPREV } } }
							check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0.9 }
						}
					}
				}
				liege = { ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				independent = yes
			}
			random_independent_ruler = {
				limit = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					war = no
					any_demesne_title = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
						check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
					}
				}
				ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV }
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { remove_trait = rebel_leader }
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.74"
		set_character_flag = issue_punishments
		FROM = {
			FROM = {
				character_event = { id = empire_wars.75 days = 1  tooltip = "TOOLTIPempire_wars.75" }
				set_character_flag = issue_punishments
			}
		}
	}
}

#Inform pardoned
letter_event = {
	id = empire_wars.76
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.76"

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		clear_event_target = empire_war_hostage
		current_heir = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					dynasty = ROOT
					is_ruler = no
					liege = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { character = FROM }
				}
				save_event_target_as = empire_war_hostage
				break = yes
			}
		}
		random_child = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
				is_ruler = no
				liege = { character = ROOT }
				NOT = { character = ROOT }
				NOT = { character = FROM }
			}
			save_event_target_as = empire_war_hostage
			break = yes
		}
		random_dynasty_member = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
				is_close_relative = ROOT
				is_ruler = no
				liege = { character = ROOT }
				NOT = { character = ROOT }
				NOT = { character = FROM }
			}
			save_event_target_as = empire_war_hostage
			break = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.76"
		event_target:empire_war_hostage = {
			move_character = FROM
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { is_in_interregnum_trigger = yes } }
				set_character_flag = interregnum_hostage
			}
			ROOT = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						prisoner = yes
						host = { character = FROM }
					}
					prisoner = no
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { event_target:empire_war_hostage = { always = yes } } }
			custom_tooltip = { text = NOSUITABLEHOSTAGE }
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = { prisoner = no }
					imprison = FROM
					set_character_flag = interregnum_prisoner
				}
				remove_character_modifier = the_oubliette
				remove_character_modifier = the_dungeon
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = house_arrest
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		clear_event_target = empire_war_hostage
		clr_character_flag = issue_punishments
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					demesne_size = 1
					trait = civil_war
					FROM = { has_landed_title = e_the_empire }
				}
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = {
						region = world_old_world_empire
					}
					gain_title = FROM
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						demesne_size = 1
						NOT = { dynasty = FROM }
					}
					any_dynasty_member = {
						limit = {
							has_character_flag = exiled_royal_family
						}
						reverse_banish = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #Removes free revocation for being a traitor
			limit = {
				OR = {
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_traitor }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion }
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_traitor }
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion }
			}
		}
	}

	after = { hidden_tooltip = { diplomatic_immunity = no } }
}

				clr_character_flag = abdication
				if = {
					limit = { is_merchant_republic = no }
					current_heir = { save_event_target_as = wealth_heir }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_merchant_republic = yes }
					family_palace = { current_heir = { save_event_target_as = wealth_heir } }
				}
				transfer_scaled_wealth = { to = event_target:wealth_heir value = all }
			}
			abdicate = yes
			recalc_succession = yes
		}
		clr_character_flag = title_revoked
		clr_character_flag = being_issued_punishment
		clr_character_flag = issue_punishments
		if = {
			limit = { prisoner = no }
			imprison = FROM
		}
		if = { #Removes free revocation for being a traitor
			limit = {
				OR = {
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_traitor }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion }
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_traitor }
				reverse_remove_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion }
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_ruler = yes }
				set_defacto_liege = FROM
			}
		}
	}

				FROM = { FROM = { job_spymaster = { intrigue = 26 } } }
			}
		}
		FROM = { set_character_flag = captured }
		FROM = { FROM = { character_event = { id = empire_wars.830 days = 10 } } }
	}
}
#Inform got away
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.81
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.81"

	show_from_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { is_consort = yes }
			consort = { remove_consort = PREV }
			clr_character_flag = no_court_invites
		}
		random_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				valid_exile_destination_ROOT_trigger = yes
				NOT = { is_liege_or_above = FROMFROMFROM }
				NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROMFROMFROM modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege } }
				NOT = { any_liege = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROMFROMFROM modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege } } }
				OR = {
					higher_tier_than = DUKE
					culture_group = ROOT
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = come_to_me
			break = yes
		}
		random_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				valid_exile_destination_ROOT_trigger = yes
				NOT = { is_liege_or_above = FROMFROMFROM }
				NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROMFROMFROM modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege } }
				NOT = { any_liege = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROMFROMFROM modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege } } }
			}
			save_event_target_as = come_to_me
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBempire_wars.81" #Merc Company
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
			age = 14
		}
		random_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				mercenary = yes
				NOT = { same_realm = FROMFROMFROM }
				is_within_diplo_range = FROMFROMFROM
				OR = {
					primary_title = {
						OR = {
							title = d_iron_shields
							title = d_ragged_standard
						}
					}
					ROOT = { dynasty = 0 }
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				any_courtier = { #Move Family
					limit = {
						is_ruler = no

						OR = {
							AND = {
								dynasty = ROOT
								NOT = { dynasty = 0 }
							}
							is_close_relative = ROOT
						}
						OR = {
							is_adult = no
							is_married = ROOT
							AND = {
								opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
								NOT = { opinion = { who = liege value = 50 } }
							}
						}
						NOT = { liege = { is_parent_of = PREV } }
						NOT = { liege = { is_married = PREV } }
						OR = {
							liege = {
								NOR = {
									dynasty = PREV
									is_close_relative = PREV
								}
							}
							is_child_of = PREV
							is_grandchild_of = PREV
						}
						NOT = { has_character_modifier = planning_claimant_adventure }
					}
					move_character = PREVPREV
				}
				move_character = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTCempire_wars.81" #random kingdom
		trigger = {
			event_target:come_to_me = { always = yes }
		}
		any_courtier = { #Move Family
			limit = {
				is_ruler = no

				OR = {
					AND = {
						dynasty = ROOT
						NOT = { dynasty = 0 }
					}
					is_close_relative = ROOT
				}
				OR = {
					is_adult = no
					is_married = ROOT
					AND = {
						opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 }
						NOT = { opinion = { who = liege value = 50 } }
					}
				}
				NOT = { liege = { is_parent_of = PREV } }
				NOT = { liege = { is_married = PREV } }
				OR = {
					liege = {
						NOR = {
							dynasty = PREV
							is_close_relative = PREV
						}
					}
					is_child_of = PREV
					is_grandchild_of = PREV
				}
				NOT = { has_character_modifier = planning_claimant_adventure }
			}
			move_character = event_target:come_to_me
		}
		move_character = event_target:come_to_me
		clear_event_target = come_to_me
	}
}

#Inform King captured
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.830
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.830"
	picture = GFX_evt_judged_by_ruler

	show_from_from = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		clear_event_target = empire_war_hostage
		FROMFROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = non_lord_revoked }	}
				current_heir = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							dynasty = PREV
							is_ruler = no
							liege = { character = PREVPREV }
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							NOT = { character = PREV }
						}
						save_event_target_as = empire_war_hostage
						break = yes
					}
				}
				random_child = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						is_ruler = no
						liege = { character = PREVPREV }
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
						NOT = { character = PREV }
					}
					save_event_target_as = empire_war_hostage
					break = yes
				}
				random_dynasty_member = {
					limit = {
						is_alive = yes
						is_close_relative = PREV
						is_ruler = no
						liege = { character = PREVPREV }
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
						NOT = { character = PREV }
					}
					save_event_target_as = empire_war_hostage
					break = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.830"
		event_target:empire_war_hostage = {
			move_character = FROM
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { is_in_interregnum_trigger = yes } }
				set_character_flag = interregnum_hostage
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_character_flag = non_lord_revoked }
					}
					any_dynasty_member = {
						limit = {
							is_alive = yes
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							is_close_relative = FROMFROM
							NOT = { is_close_relative = ROOT }
						}
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_wiped_out_my_family
							years = 25
						}
					}
				}
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = { id = 154 } #on_executed event
				}
				death = {
					death_reason = death_execution
					killer = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { FROM = { NOT = { age = 16 } } }
			}
			FROM = {
				FROM = {
					any_dynasty_member = {
						limit = {
							is_alive = yes
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							is_close_relative = FROMFROM
						}
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_executed_child
							years = 25
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Rebel Leader resolution, deals with defeated emperor
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.86
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.86"
	picture = GFX_evt_judged_by_ruler

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = { #Is the emperor
				trait = civil_war
				OR = { #Must have reason to judge
					AND = {
						NOT = { tier = EMPEROR } #implies usurped
						FROM = {
							tier = EMPEROR
								reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_usurped_title }
						}
					}
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_vengeance }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROMFROM modifier = opinion_vengeance }
					AND = {
						prisoner = yes
						host = { character = FROM }
					}
				}
			}
			AND = { #Any other defenders must be vassal of victor
				demesne_size = 1
				FROM = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					OR = {
						is_vassal_or_below = ROOT
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = EMPEROR
							ROOT = {
								primary_title = {
									lower_tier_than = EMPEROR
									is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }
								}
							}
							check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
				NOT = { has_character_flag = independant }
				NOT = { any_liege = { has_character_flag = independant NOT = { character = FROM } } }
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = { #Special effects for defeated 'emperor'
			limit = {
				trait = civil_war
			}
			any_courtier = { #Remove descendants of rebel victor from potential judgement
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = former_royal_courtier
					OR = {
						is_close_relative = ROOT
						dynasty = ROOT
					}
					OR = {
						is_child_of = FROM
						is_married = FROM
						father_even_if_dead = { is_child_of = FROM }
						mother_even_if_dead = { is_child_of = FROM }
					}
					NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_vengeance } }
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
				}
				clr_character_flag = former_royal_courtier
			}
			#If enemy has usurped the emperor's title, change orientation of former emperor's allies and manage flags
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
					FROM = {
						tier = EMPEROR
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_usurped_title }
					}
				}

				#Manage traits/flags
				FROM = { #Victor
					add_trait = civil_war
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { NOT = { trait = rebel_leader } } }
						remove_trait = rebel_leader
					}
					if = { #If old emperor was at war with another emperor reset connections
						limit = { trait = rebel_leader }
						any_independent_ruler = {
							limit = {
								tier = EMPEROR
								NOT = { character = ROOT }
								NOT = { character = PREV }
								reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_emperor_rebel_leader }
							}
							reverse_opinion = { who = PREV modifier = opinion_emperor_rebel_leader years = 25 }
						}
						any_independent_ruler = {
							limit = {
								tier = EMPEROR
								NOT = { character = ROOT }
								NOT = { character = PREV }
								has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_emperor_rebel_leader }
							}
							opinion = { who = PREV modifier = opinion_emperor_rebel_leader years = 25 }
						}
					}
				}
				any_independent_ruler = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = supporting_king
						has_opinion_modifier = { modifier = opinion_with_king who = ROOT }
					}
					clr_character_flag = supporting_king
					set_character_flag = neutral
					any_vassal = {
						clr_character_flag = supporting_king
						set_character_flag = neutral
					}
				}
				any_playable_ruler = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = against_king
						has_opinion_modifier = { modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader who = FROM }
					}
					clr_character_flag = against_king
					set_character_flag = supporting_king
					any_vassal = {
						clr_character_flag = against_king
						set_character_flag = supporting_king
					}
					remove_opinion = { modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader who = FROM }
					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_king
						who = FROM
						years = 100
					}
				}

				any_courtier = { #Any non hidden relatives stand judgement
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = former_royal_courtier
						OR = {
							NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
							AND = {
								prisoner = yes
								host = { character = ROOT_FROM }
							}
						}
						OR = {
							dynasty = ROOT
							is_close_relative = ROOT
						}
						OR = {
							prisoner = no
							host = { character = ROOT_FROM }
							host = { character = ROOT }
						}
						NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
						OR = {
							NOT = { has_character_flag = exiled_royal_family }
							host = { character = ROOT_FROM }
						}
					}
					clr_character_flag = former_royal_courtier
					set_character_flag = judge_me
				}
				any_courtier = { #Any hidden relatives may go into exile
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = former_royal_courtier
						NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
						is_inaccessible_trigger = yes
						OR = {
							is_close_relative = ROOT
							dynasty = ROOT
						}
					}
					clr_character_flag = former_royal_courtier
					remove_trait = in_hiding
					set_character_flag = exiled_royal_family
				}
			}
			if = { #If the enemy desires vengeance judge entire family
				limit = { FROM = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_vengeance } } }
				any_courtier = { #Any non-hidden relatives stand judgement
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = former_royal_courtier
						OR = {
							NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
							AND = {
								prisoner = yes
								host = { character = ROOT_FROM }
							}
						}
						OR = {
							dynasty = ROOT
							is_close_relative = ROOT
						}
						NOR = {
							is_child_of = FROM
							father_even_if_dead = { is_child_of = FROM }
							mother_even_if_dead = { is_child_of = FROM }
						}
						NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
						OR = {
							NOT = { has_character_flag = exiled_royal_family }
							host = { character = ROOT_FROM }
						}
					}
					clr_character_flag = former_royal_courtier
					set_character_flag = judge_me
				}
			}
			any_courtier = { #Also judge particular courtiers for vengeance
				limit = {
					has_character_flag = former_royal_courtier
					OR = {
						NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
						AND = {
							prisoner = yes
							host = { character = ROOT_FROM }
						}
					}
					NOT = { demesne_size = 1 }
					OR = {
						NOT = { has_character_flag = exiled_royal_family }
						host = { character = ROOT_FROM }
					}
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_vengeance }
				}
				clr_character_flag = former_royal_courtier
				set_character_flag = judge_me
			}
			any_courtier = { #Clear the rest
				limit = { has_character_flag = former_royal_courtier }
				clr_character_flag = former_royal_courtier
			}
			if = {
				limit = { #if ROOT is hidden send into exile as well
					trait = in_hiding
					is_ruler = no
				}
				set_character_flag = exiled_royal_family
				remove_trait = in_hiding
				clr_character_flag = judge_me
				clr_character_flag = former_royal_courtier
				prisoner = no
			}
			clr_character_flag = former_royal_courtier
		}
		if = {
			limit = { war = no }
			if = {
				limit = {
					lower_tier_than = KING
					primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 1 } }
					NOT = { liege = { character = FROM } }
				}
				random_playable_ruler = {
					limit = {
						liege = {
							higher_tier_than = DUKE
							any_demesne_title = {
								higher_tier_than = DUKE
								ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" which = PREVPREV } } }
								check_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0.9 }
							}
						}
					}
					liege = { ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV } }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					independent = yes
				}
				random_independent_ruler = {
					limit = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						war = no
						any_demesne_title = {
							tier = EMPEROR
							ROOT = { primary_title = { is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV } } }
							check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
						}
					}
					ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.86"
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_character_flag = exiled_pretender }
			}
			set_character_flag = issue_punishments
			FROM = {
				character_event = { id = empire_wars.87 tooltip = "TOOLTIPempire_wars.75" }
				set_character_flag = issue_punishments
			}
		}
	}
}

#Vassal is harbouring exiled pretender
character_event  = {
	id = empire_wars.96
	desc = "EVTDESCempire_wars.96"

	only_independent = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tier = EMPEROR
		any_demesne_title = {
			tier = EMPEROR
			any_claimant = {
				is_ruler = no
				is_liege_or_above = ROOT
				NOT = { liege = { character = ROOT } }
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = exiled_royal_family
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_exiled_pretender
					}
				}
				NOT = { dynasty = ROOT }
				NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_merciful } }
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_realm_character = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = no
				NOT = { liege = { character = ROOT } }
				any_claim = { tier = EMPEROR holder_scope = { character = ROOT } }
				OR = {
					has_character_flag = exiled_royal_family
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_exiled_pretender
					}
				}
				NOT = { dynasty = ROOT }
				NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_merciful } }
			}
			save_event_target_as = exiled_target
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTAempire_wars.96"  #Demand they hand them over
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = lunatic
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = paranoid
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = cruel
			}
		}
		event_target:exiled_target = {
			custom_tooltip = { text = TOOLTIPempire_wars.96 }
			liege = { tooltip = { show_portrait = yes } }
			hidden_tooltip = { liege = { letter_event = { id = empire_wars.97 days = 4 } } }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBempire_wars.96"  #Leave them be
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = slothful
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = trusting
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = kind
			}
		}
		event_target:exiled_target = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_merciful
				who = ROOT
				years = 20
			}
		}
	}
}

				}
				move_character = FROM
				imprison = FROM
				opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_gave_me_up
					who = ROOT
					years = 10
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { letter_event = { id = empire_wars.98 } } }
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTBempire_wars.97"  #Never!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = diligent
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_strong_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = arbitrary
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				tier = KING
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				event_target:exiled_target = {
					dynasty = ROOT
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				event_target:exiled_target = {
					is_married = ROOT
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				trait = honorable
				event_target:exiled_target = {
					OR = {
						is_married = ROOT
						dynasty = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clr_global_flag = war_cooldown_period
		if = {
			limit = { liege = { NOT = { character = FROM } } }
			hidden_tooltip = { set_defacto_liege = FROM }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { letter_event = { id = empire_wars.99 } } }
		event_target:exiled_target = {
			if = { #Check war is actually possible
				limit = {
						can_press_claims_trigger = yes
				}
				character_event = { id = empire_wars.100 tooltip = TOOLTIPempire_wars.100 days = 1 }
			}
			if = { #If not, try another courtier
				limit = {
						can_press_claims_trigger = no
				}
				random_courtier = {
					limit = {
						liege = { character = ROOT }
						any_claim = { tier = EMPEROR holder_scope = { character = FROM } }
						OR = {
							dynasty = PREV
							is_close_relative = PREV
						}
							can_press_claims_trigger = yes
					}
					character_event = { id = empire_wars.100 tooltip = TOOLTIPempire_wars.100 days = 1 }
				}
				#Else just rebel
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							any_courtier = {
								liege = { character = ROOT }
								any_claim = { tier = EMPEROR holder_scope = { character = FROM } }
								OR = {
									dynasty = PREV
									is_close_relative = PREV
								}
									can_press_claims_trigger = yes
							}
						}
					}
					FROM = {
						reverse_war = {
							target = ROOT
							casus_belli = overthrow_ruler
						}
						character_event = { id = 45431 } #other vassals may join
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### Maintaining the Council ###
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.101
	desc = EVTDESCempire_wars.101
	picture = GFX_evt_council

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { # Can't reappoint rulers that are no longer your vassal for whatever reason or already a councillor
		any_opinion_modifier_target = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_castellan }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_chancellor }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_marshal }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_treasurer }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_spymaster }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_learned }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_priest }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor }
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { liege = { character = ROOT } }
					is_councillor = yes
					is_voter = yes
					prisoner = yes
					trait = incapable
					is_inaccessible_trigger = yes
					has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_fired_from_council }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_traitor }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion }
				}
			}
			set_character_flag = invalid_councillor
		}
		clr_character_flag = empire_war_reappointing_council
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAempire_wars.101 # I will reapoint the old council
			trigger = {
				any_opinion_modifier_target = {
					OR = {
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_castellan }

						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_priest }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_commander }

				}
			}
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPCempire_wars.101 # I will decide my new council
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					any_opinion_modifier_target = {
						OR = {
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_castellan }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_chancellor }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_marshal }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_treasurer }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_spymaster }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_learned }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_priest }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor }
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_commander }
						}
						NOT = { has_character_flag = invalid_councillor }

				NOT = { has_character_flag = invalid_councillor }
			}

		name = EVTOPBempire_wars.101

					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_priest }

						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_spymaster }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_learned }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_priest }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor }
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_commander }
					}
				}
				reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_castellan }
				reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_chancellor }
				reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_marshal }
				reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_treasurer }
				reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_spymaster }
				reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_learned }
				reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_priest }
				reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor }
				reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_commander }
			}
		}
	}
}
# Player offered their old council position back
letter_event = {
	id = empire_wars.102
	desc = EVTDESCempire_wars.102

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { liege = { character = FROM } }

	option = { # Of course I want my old job back
		name = EVTOPTAempire_wars.102
		if = {
			limit = {
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_castellan }
			}
			give_job_title = job_castellan
			hidden_tooltip = { reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_castellan } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_chancellor }
			}
			give_job_title = job_chancellor
			hidden_tooltip = { reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_chancellor } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_marshal }
			}
			give_job_title = job_marshal
			hidden_tooltip = { reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_marshal } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_treasurer }
			}
			give_job_title = job_treasurer
			hidden_tooltip = { reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_treasurer } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_spymaster }
			}
			give_job_title = job_spymaster
			hidden_tooltip = { reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_spymaster } }
		}
		if = {

			}
			give_job_title = job_physician
			hidden_tooltip = { reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_learned } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_priest }
			}
			give_job_title = job_spiritual
			hidden_tooltip = { reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_priest } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor }
			}
			#Advisors
			if = {
				limit = { has_dlc = "Zeus" }
				hidden_tooltip = {
					FROM = {
						random_opinion_modifier_target = {
							limit = {
								reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor }
							}
							FROM = {
								random_realm_character = {
									limit = {
										liege = { character = FROM }
										has_minor_title = title_councilmember_king
										NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor } }
									}
									remove_title = title_councilmember_king
									PREVPREV = { give_minor_title = title_councilmember_king }
								}
							}
						}
						random_opinion_modifier_target = {
							limit = {
								reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor }
							}
							FROM = {
								random_realm_character = {
									limit = {
										liege = { character = FROM }
										has_minor_title = title_councilmember_emperor
										NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor } }
									}
									remove_title = title_councilmember_emperor
									PREVPREV = { give_minor_title = title_councilmember_emperor }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_dlc = "Zeus" } }
				hidden_tooltip = {
					FROM = {
						random_opinion_modifier_target = {
							limit = {
								reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor }
							}
							FROM = {
								if = {
									limit = {
										any_realm_character = {
											liege = { character = FROM }
											has_minor_title = title_small_council_advisor
											count = 3
										}
									}
									random_realm_character = {
										limit = {
											liege = { character = FROM }
											has_minor_title = title_small_council_advisor
											NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor } }
										}
										remove_title = title_small_council_advisor
									}
								}
							}
							give_minor_title = title_small_council_advisor
						}
						random_opinion_modifier_target = {
							limit = {
								reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor }
							}
							FROM = {
								if = {
									limit = {
										any_realm_character = {
											liege = { character = FROM }
											has_minor_title = title_small_council_advisor
											count = 3
										}
									}
									random_realm_character = {
										limit = {
											liege = { character = FROM }
											has_minor_title = title_small_council_advisor
											NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor } }
										}
										remove_title = title_small_council_advisor
									}
								}
							}
							give_minor_title = title_small_council_advisor
						}
						random_opinion_modifier_target = {
							limit = {
								reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor }
							}
							FROM = {
								if = {
									limit = {
										any_realm_character = {
											liege = { character = FROM }
											has_minor_title = title_small_council_advisor
											count = 3
										}
									}
									random_realm_character = {
										limit = {
											liege = { character = FROM }
											has_minor_title = title_small_council_advisor
											NOT = { reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor } }
										}
										remove_title = title_small_council_advisor
									}
								}
							}
							give_minor_title = title_small_council_advisor
						}
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor } }
		}
		FROM = { letter_event = { id = empire_wars.103 tooltip = TOOLTIPempire_wars.102 } }
	}
	option = { # I am alright thanks
		name = EVTOPTBempire_wars.102
		FROM = {
			letter_event = { id = empire_wars.103 tooltip = TOOLTIPBempire_wars.102 }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_castellan }
			reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_chancellor }
			reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_marshal }
			reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_treasurer }
			reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_spymaster }
			reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_learned }
			reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_priest }
			reverse_remove_opinion  = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_pre_empire_war_advisor }
		}
	}

# FROM is informed whether the player accepted or not
letter_event = {
	id = empire_wars.103

	desc = { # Accepted
		text = EVTDESACempire_wars.103
		trigger = { FROM = { is_councillor = yes } }
	}
	desc = { # Rejected
		text = EVTDESBCempire_wars.103
		trigger = { FROM = { is_councillor = no } }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTAempire_wars.103
			trigger = { FROM = { is_councillor = yes } }
		}
		name = {
			text = EVTOPTBempire_wars.103
			trigger = { FROM = { is_councillor = no } }
		}
	}
}
# Check player actually sends help in the war
character_event = {
	id = empire_wars.105
	desc = EVTDESACempire_wars.105
	picture = GFX_evt_war_planning

	is_triggered_only = yes
	ai = no
	only_independent = yes
	war = yes

	trigger = {
		any_opinion_modifier_target = {
			is_ruler = yes
			war = yes
			NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
			OR = {
				AND = {
					tier = EMPEROR
					trait = civil_war
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_with_king
					}
				}
				AND = {
					trait = rebel_leader
					is_ruler = yes
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
					}
				}
			}
			any_war = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						attacker = { character = PREVPREV }
						defender = { war_with = ROOT }
					}
					AND = {
						defender = { character = PREVPREV }
						attacker = { war_with = ROOT }
					}
				}
				days_since_last_hostile_action = {
					who = ROOT     # The character whose activity is being checked
					days = 730    # Number of days since last battle participation or offensive siege (2 years)
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				any_war = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							attacker = { character = PREVPREV }
							defender = { war_with = ROOT }
						}
						AND = {
							defender = { character = PREVPREV }
							attacker = { war_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						days_since_last_hostile_action = {
							who = ROOT     # The character whose activity is being checked
							days = 730    # Number of days since last battle participation or offensive siege (2 years)
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_nickname = no }
			random_list = {
				100 = { }
				10 = { set_character_flag = nick_the_latecomer }
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR =  {
							is_female = yes
							is_feudal = no
						}
					}
					set_character_flag = nick_the_late_lord
				}
				10 = { set_character_flag = nick_the_late }
				10 = { set_character_flag = nick_the_cautious }
				10 = { set_character_flag = nick_the_indecisive }
				10 = { set_character_flag = nick_the_ditherer }
				10 = { set_character_flag = nick_the_waverer }
				10 = { set_character_flag = nick_the_hesitant }
			}
		}
		random_opinion_modifier_target = {
			limit = {
				is_ruler = yes
				war = yes
				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						trait = civil_war
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_with_king
						}
					}
					AND = {
						trait = rebel_leader
						is_ruler = yes
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						}
					}
				}
				any_war = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							attacker = { character = PREVPREV }
							defender = { war_with = ROOT }
						}
						AND = {
							defender = { character = PREVPREV }
							attacker = { war_with = ROOT }
						}
					}
					days_since_last_hostile_action = {
						who = ROOT     # The character whose activity is being checked
						days = 730    # Number of days since last battle participation or offensive siege (2 years)
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					any_war = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								attacker = { character = PREVPREV }
								defender = { war_with = ROOT }
							}
							AND = {
								defender = { character = PREVPREV }
								attacker = { war_with = ROOT }
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							days_since_last_hostile_action = {
								who = ROOT     # The character whose activity is being checked
								days = 730    # Number of days since last battle participation or offensive siege (2 years)
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = disgruntled_ally
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAempire_wars.105
		event_target:disgruntled_ally = {
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_dithered
				years = 10
				multiplier = 2
			}
		}
		prestige = -100
		if = { #If this happens more than once, add dishonour
			limit = { has_character_flag = empire_war_known_ditherer }
			change_variable = { which = "dishonorable" value = 10 }
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = maintenance.3 } } #dishonour trait
		}
		set_character_flag = empire_war_known_ditherer
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = nick_the_latecomer }
			clr_character_flag = nick_the_latecomer
			give_nickname = nick_the_latecomer
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = nick_the_late }
			clr_character_flag = nick_the_late
			give_nickname = nick_the_late
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = nick_the_cautious }
			clr_character_flag = nick_the_cautious
			give_nickname = nick_the_cautious
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = nick_the_indecisive }
			clr_character_flag = nick_the_indecisive
			give_nickname = nick_the_indecisive
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = nick_the_ditherer }
			clr_character_flag = nick_the_ditherer
			give_nickname = nick_the_ditherer
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = nick_the_waverer }
			clr_character_flag = nick_the_waverer
			give_nickname = nick_the_waverer
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag = nick_the_hesitant }
			clr_character_flag = nick_the_hesitant
			give_nickname = nick_the_hesitant
		}
	}
}
